atra yatpareShAM dUShaNaM "maN^galasya vAkyArthe samanvayAbhAvAt.h' iti | "tathA hi | padArtha eva hi vAkyArthe samanvIyate | sa cha vAchyo vA lakShyo vA | na cheha maN^galamathashabdasya vAchyaM lakShyaM vA | kintu mR^idaN^gadhvanivadathashabdasya kAryam.h | nacha kAryaj~nApyayorvAkyArthe samanvayaH shAbde vyavahAre dR^iShyaH' | "astu vA maN^galasya padArthatvam.h | tathA.api na vAkyArthe samanvayaH | tathAhi | na tAvanmaN^galaM brahmajij~nAsAyAH kartR^ikarmakaraNabhAvena vAkyArthe.anveti | kartrAdyanyatamabhAve pramANAbhAvAt.h | kArakAntarANAM vidyamAnatvAchcha | nApi sAmAnAdhikaraNyena anvayaH | jij~nAsA maN^galamiti prashaMsAparatayA arthavAdatvaprasaN^gAt.h' iti | tadetenApAstaM bhavati | asmAbhirapyAnantaryAbhidheyo.athashabdaH shrutyA maN^galaprayojana ityaN^gIkArAt.h | nanvatra sUtrAdAvoN^kAra eva na vidyate | tatkathamuchyate tArAthamUlatvati | yadyapi shiShyairadh.hyetR^ibhiH uchchAryamANo.adhyakShasiddhastathApi nAyaM sUtrAvayavaH | lakShaNAntarAbhAve satyasaMhitatayA sampAThe akhilaiH paThyamAnatvAt.h | vedAdhyayanopakrame adhyetR^ibhiruchchAryamANoN^kAravat.h | anyathA.athashabdavatsaMhitatayA nirdishyeta | nacha dR^iShyAntaH sAdhyavikalaH | adhyayanopakramavirativaichityeNa tattatsthAnaparityAgenAnyAnyasthAne.akhilaiH paThyamAnasya vedavAkyAnavayavatAyAH suprasiddhatvAt.h | anyathA.adhyayanopakramavirativaichitye.api OM iti brahmetyAdivanniyatasthAnatayA pAThaprasaN^gAt.h | pakShasapakShayorAdAvuchchAraNaM tu prAN^mukhatvAdivadadhyayananiyamAntargatamadhyetR^ibhiranuShThIyata ityastu | evaMchAyamoN^kAraH sUtrakR^itA maN^galArthatayA sUtrAdAvupanibaddha ityanupapannamityata Aha- sarvatra iti || akhilaiH sUtrapAThakaiH yatpR^ithagasaMhitatayoN^kriyate tatsarvatra sUtreShvanugatatvenAbhilaShitena nimittenopapadyate | 
etadukttaM bhavati | sarvANi hi sUtrANi pratyekamanekavedavAkyavichAraparatvAdavAntarabrahmavidyAH | "sravatyanoN^kR^itaM brahma parastAchcha vishIryate' iti shrautArthavAdasAmarthyAtsarvAsvapi brahmavidyAsvAdyantayoroN^kArasyohaH kartavya iti gamyate | na chohyamAnaM vAkyAtpR^ithagiti shakyate vakttum.h | mantreShvapyUhyamAnasyAmantrAvayavatvaprasaN^gAt.h | tatashcha patisUtramAdyantayoruchchAraNe gauravaM syAdityAdAvevoN^kAro.adhikR^itatvenochchAryate | tasya saMhitatayA nirdeshe prathamasUtrAvayava evAyaM vij~nAyeta | tanmA vij~nAyIti shiShyaiH pR^ithagoN^kriyate | nacha vyAkhyAnato.apyadhikAro j~nAyata iti vyarthaM pR^ithakkaraNamiti vAchyam.h | antaraN^gaj~nApakAbhAva eva bahiraN^gasyAnveShaNIyatvAditi | tadanenAsaMhitatayA nirdeshe nimittAntaraM vadatA hetoranyathAsiddhirukttA bhavati | 
nanu cha shrautArthavAdabalenAdyantayoroN^kArasyoho vA prAN^mukhatvAdivadbahirbhUtasyaiva uchchAraNaM vA vidheyatvena kalpyamiti sandihyate | satyam.h | sandehe.api tayA praNADyAnumAnasya sandigdhAnyathAsiddhayA.apyAbhAsatvameva | vakShyamANanyAyenoN^kArArthasya prathamasUtravAkyArthe samanvayena nishchayopapattau bAdhitaviShayaM chAnumAnamiti | athavA dR^iShyAntadUShaNamanena kriyate | tathAhi | akhilairvedapAThakaiH pR^ithagrUpAntareNa sthAnavyatyAsena yadoN^kriyate tadukttanyAyenAdAvuchchAraNenaiva labdhena sarvatrAnugatatvena kAraNenaivopapadyata ityanena dR^iShyAnte sAdhakasya hetoranyathAsiddhirukttA | tathAcha dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavikalateti | evamanumAne niraste nirapavAdenAdAvuchchAraNenoN^kArasya prathamasUtrAvayavatAsiddhAvukttamupapannam.h | tadevaM siddhe shAstravyAkhyeyatve prekShAvatpravR^ittiviShayasyaiva ArambhaNIyatvAtprayojanAbhidheyasambandhavatyeva cha prekShAvatAM pravR^itterArambhaNIyatAsiddhaye prekShAvataH pravartayituM prayojanAdyabhisambandhaM pratipAdayataH prathamasUtrasya vyAkhyAmotatvavAchItyAdinA Arabhate | 
nanu brahmaj~nAnasya mokShahetutA yadi shAstrapravR^itteH prAgeva pramANAntarasiddhA vyarthaM tadA tadabhidhAnaM shAstre | pramANAntarasiddhe kvachidupadeshAnapekShaNAt.h | athehaiva tannishchayastadA pravR^ittau prayojanAdinishchayo nishchite cha prayojanAdau pravR^ittirityanyonyAshrayatvam.h | atha prathamasUtrAttannishchayaH | tatraiva 
kathaM pravR^ittiH | tadarthaM cha prayojanAntarAbhidhAne.anavasthA | evameva tatra pravR^ittAvuttaratrApi tathAtvaprasaN^gAdanarthakaM sUtre prayojanAdyabhidhAnamiti | uchyate | trividhA hi puMsAM chittavR^ittiH | anubhava ichChA prayatnashcha | tatra sAdhanagocharAvichChAprayatnau pravR^ittiriti uchyete | na tvanubhavo nApi phalagocharechChA | yena tayorapi prayojananishchayApekShA syAt.h | nahi upekShaNIyaM niShprayojanamiti nAnubhUyate | nApi sukhaM prayojanAntararahitamiti neShyate | nacha mumukShuNA anapekShite svarge yAgAdikaM tatsAdhanatayA nAnubhUyate | puruShAtharsAdhane tu ichChAlakShaNA prayatnalakShaNA vA pravR^ittistathA na svarasasiddhA | nahi kashchitkShutprahANAdikamananusandhAya bhokttumichChati prayatate vA | tasmAdyo yatra pravartanIyaH sa tatprayojanAdikaM darshayitvaiva iti sArthakaM sUtre prayojanAdyabhidhAnam.h | 
ukttaM cha prayojanAdikaM shrotA kataM shraddadhItAshraddadhAnashcha kathaM pravatareteti punaravashiShyate | tatraike samAdhAnamAhuH | avagatasUtrakArAptabhAvastAvattadvachanAdeva shraddhAsyati | pravR^ittiriti chAtisthavIyaH | nahi kashchitprayojanAdisandehe.atimahAyAsasAdhye pravartate prAgukttAnarthaparamparAshcha kathaM na shaN^keta | tasmAnnedaM prayojanAdyupadeshamAtraM kintu shrautasya adhyayanavidhyAdivadasyApyata evArambhaNIyatvasiddhernAnavasthAdidoSho.apIti | 
kaH punarasya sUtrasya prasaN^gaH | uchyate | prAripsitatayA hi buddhisannihitaM shAstraM sUtrakArasya | tatra saMshayaH kimidamArambhaNIyaM na veti | upalabhyante khalUbhayavidhAnyapi vAkyAni | vAkyaM chedam.h | nacha visheSho dR^ishyate | yenAnyatarapakShanishchayaH syAt.h | nanu kasyAyaM saMshayaH | na tAvatsUtrakArasya | avagatavisheShatvAt.h | anyathA nirNAyakasUtrapraNayanAnupapatteH | nApi parasya | pareNAdyApi shAstrasyAnupalabdhatvAt.h | anupalabdhe cha samAnadharmadarshanAdyayogena saMshayotpAdAnupapatteH | maivam.h | yadIdaM shAstraM pareNopalabhyeta tadokttasandehakAraNopapattau prayojanArthitvena visheShasmR^itimataivaM sandihyeteti sUtrakR^ita eva parakIyasambhAvitasaMshayAharaNopapatteH |

vichAreNa shrutyarthasya AdyApyanirNItatvena saMshayAspadatvAt.h | tatra tAvajjij~nAsA na kartavyeti prAptam.h | kutaH | viShayaprayojanasambandhAdhikArilakShaNAnubandhavidhuratvAt.h | kartavyatA yathokttam.h | "avij~nAtatattve.arthe kAraNopapattitastattvaj~nAnArthamUhastarkaH' iti | niShpAditakriye cha karmaNyavisheShAdhAyinaH sAdhanasya sAdhananyAyAtipAtaH | nApyasau jij~nAsitaH kasmaichana prayojanAya kalpate | evaMvidhe chAdhikArI dUrotsAritaH | yato.arthI samartho vidvAnadhikriyate | nachaitAdR^ishe.arthe.arthitA sambhavati | dharmAdilakShaNastvanAtmA shAstrAntarAdinaiva nirNItaH | nishchIyata iti chet.h | evaM tarhi tata eva na jij~nAsyaH | ata evAnAditastadIyatattvaj~nAne vidyamAne.api iShyAniShyaprAptiparihArayoradarshanAnnAsau jij~nAsitaH kasyachitprayojanasyeShye | 
nanvayaM kartA bhokttA doShasaMsargI chAhaMpratyaye prakAshate | tadviparItastu shrutipratipAditaH pratipattavyo.ato jij~nAseti chet.h | evaM tarhi jaradgavAdivAkyavatpAvakashaityAnumAnavachcha pratItivirodhena shrutijij~nAsayorAbhAsatApAtaH | ata eva na parAtmA jij~nAsyaH | tasya prANAdiliN^gairavagatatvAt.h | saiva jij~nAseti chenna | tasyA laukikapravedanIyatvena shAstrAvyutpAdanIyatvAt.h | na khalu bAlakaH stanapAneShyasAdhanatvAnumAne shAstravyutpAdanamapekShate | yatkvachichChAstre.api laukikapravedanIyArthavyutpAdanamanuvAdo.asau na punaH sa eva pradhAnavyApAraH | IshvaraviShayA jij~nAsA bhaviShyatIti chenna | tasyaivAbhAvAt.h | na chaivamIshvarAdipadAnAmAnarthakyenApadatvaprasaN^ga iti vAchyam.h | teShAM kathaJNchijjIvaviShayatopapatteH | so.api hi svasharIrendriyAdInAmIShye | pratItArthatvopapattAvapratItArthatvakalpanAyAM gauravaprasaN^gAt.h | jIvasya chAhamiti svaprakAshatayA svaprakAshaj~nAnAshrayatayA mAnasapratyakShavedyatayA vA siddhatvena na jij~nAsAviShayatvamityukttam.h | 
kiJNcheshvaraH pramito na vA | nobhayathApi jij~nAsA sambhavati | neti pakShe anugrAhyapramANAbhAvena jij~nAsAyAstarkatvavyAghAtAt.h | kAraNopapattita iti hi ukttam.h | pramAkaraNasya pramANasyopapattiranugrahastatkaraNenetyatharH | nacha buddhAvanArUDhaM shakyaM jij~nAsitum.h | pramitatve tu nishchitatvAdeva | nachaivaM sakalatarkAnupapattiprasaN^gena vyAghAtaH | sAmAnyataH pratItau visheShe tadavakAshAt.h | na chAtra tathAtvaM pashyAmaH | kiJNcheshvare pramANaM bhavanna tAvatpratyakSham.h | tasyApAtatastadabhAvAvedakatvAt.h | nApyanumAnam.h | tatpratibaddhaliN^gAbhAvAt.h | Agamastu kAryaniShTho na niShpannasvarUpamIshvaraM shaknotyavagamayitum.h | na chAnyatpramANamasti yanmImAMsayA anugR^ihyeta | kiJNchAgamo.api bhavanveda eva vakttavyaH | anyasyAnAshaN^kanIyatvAtpAratantAchcha | vedasya pauruSheyatvApauruSheyatvayoH kAraNAbhAvena prAmANyameva durlabham.h | svataH prAmANyAN^gIkAre tu vedaviruddhAnAmapi shAkyAdivachasAM tathAtvApAtena punarvedApramANyatAdavasthyam.h | kiJNcha shabdasyaiva prAmANyaM durghaTamarthasaMsparshashUnyatvAt.h | vAkyArthapratyAyanaprakArAnirUpaNAchcha | kutastadvisheShasya vedasya | 
prayojanaM cheshvarajij~nAsayA abhyudayo vA sy.hA mokSho vA | nAdyaH | tasya dharmAdilaghUpAyasAdhyasya shAstrAntaraprayojanatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | tasyApyapAma somamityAdyAgamena laghUpAyAntarasAdhyatAvagamAt.h | nachaikasyaiva karmaNo.abhyudayaniHshreyasahetutvaM viruddham.h | phalAbhisandhyAdibhAvAbhAvAbhyAM visheShopapatteH | jij~nAsA cha mokShasAdhanaM bhavantI kiM sAkShAduta j~nAnadvAreNa | nAdyaH | dR^iShyAdR^iShyatyAgakalpanAprasaN^gAt.h | na dvitIyaH | karmaNA j~nAnamAtanotItyAgamena j~nAnasya laghUpAyAntarasAdhyatAdhyavasAyAt.h | j~nAnasyApi sAkShAnmokShahetutvAbhyupagame.adR^iShyakalpanaiva | na cheshvaraprasAdadvArA | j~nAnasya prasAdahetutAyAH kvApyadR^iShyatvAt.h | "tatkarma haritoShaM yat.h' ityAdinA tatprasAdasya karmAdyalpopAyasAdhyatApratIteshcha | kiJNchAyamAtmA.avidyAkalpito bandhastadvidyayaiva nivR^ittimarhati | shukttikA.avidyAkalpitaM rajatamiva shukttividyayA | tatkuto bandhanivR^ittilakShaNe mokShe parameshvaraprasAdasyopayogaH | kutastarAM tajj~nAnasya kutastamAM cha tajjij~nAsAyAH | atha parAmArtha evAyaM bandhastarhi na j~nAnena nivarteta | nacha satyasyAnAderAtmasvarUpamAtrAnubandhino bandhasyAtmasvarUpasyeva kenApi nivR^ittiryukttA | api cha mukttasya sharIrendriyaviShayAdisaMsarge mukttatvavyAghAtaH | duHkhAdiprasaN^gashcha | kAraNasAmagrIsadbhAvAt.h | tathAchAbhyudayatulyatayokttadoShaH | sharIrAdyabhAve cha tatsAdhyasukhAbhAvena kasyApi tatrArthitAnupapatteranadhikArikaM shAstramApadyeta | ko hi svasthAtmA sahasA sukhatatsAdhane hAtumutsahate | tadevaM viShayAdyanubandhavidhuratvAnna jij~nAsA kartavyA | tadvidhayo.api na pramANam.h | shAstraM chedamanArambhaNIyamiti prApte sUtrayAmAsa bhagavAnAchAryaH- OM athAto brahmajij~nAseti ||

atrochyate | satyamevam.h | tathA.api pratibandhanivR^ittau satyAmeva nirNaya iti pratibandhakanirAsahetorapi vichArasyopachAreNa nirNayahetutvAdupapannamIshvaraviShayatvam.h | etenaitadapi nirastam.h | Ishvarasya vedapramANakatve tata eva nishchitatvAtkiM mImAMsayeti | yukttivAkyAbhAsajanitavipratipattipratibandhasyokttatvAt.h | tathA hi | vedaprAmANyamevAnaN^gIkurvANAH kechidIshvara eva nAstIti pratipannAH | apare tu tadaN^gIkR^ityApi tadvAchinAM padAnAM jIvAdiviShayatAM vyAkurvantastadabhAvamasthitAH | anye tu punarastIshvaraH kintu paramArthato nirguNa eveti saN^girante | eke tu saguNo.api na jagataH kAraNamapi tUdAsIna evetyAtiShThante | kechitkAraNatve.apyupAdAnamityabhyupayanti | nimittamAtratve.api katipayaguNaM guNebhyo bhinnamanye manyante | itare tu bhinnAbhinnamupagatavantaH | kechidvigrahavantamityevamAdyAsvanekAsu vipratipattiShu satIShu tattvaj~nAnakaraNAdapi vedAttadanutpattau tadapanodanadvAreNa vedetikartavyatArUpA jij~nAsA kartavyeti | 
tatra tAvadbrahmaNo jij~nAsA brahmajij~nAseti ShaShThIsamAso na punardharmAya jij~nAsetivachchaturthIsamAsaH | tAdarthyasamAse prakR^itigrahaNaM kartavyamiti vArtikakR^itA prakR^itivikArabhAva eva chaturthIsamAsasya niyamitatvAt.h | tathaivodAharaNaM yUpAya dAru yUpadArviti | prakR^itivikArabhAvarahiteShu chAshvaghAsAdiShvashvaghAsAdayaH ShaShThIsamAsA bhavantIti prativihitam.h | nachAtra prakR^itivikArabhAvo.asti | ShaShThIsamAse.api kechichCheShe ShaShThIti pratipannAH | kechitkarmaNIti | tatra karmaNi ShaShThIparigrahAya jij~nAsya ityakttam.h | kR^ityAnAM karmaNi smaraNAt.h | anyathA jij~nAsAsyetyavakShyat.h | jij~nAsA khalu karmApekShA vinA karmaNA na j~nAtuM shakyA na tu sambandhinaM vineti karmaNaH prAdhAnyAttadeva vakttavyam.h | sambandhisAmAnyokttavarthAtkarmApi labhyata iti chenna | sAkShAtpratItaparityAgenArthalabhyasvIkArasya vaiyarthyAt.h | evaM sati lakShaNAdijij~nAsA.api pratij~nAtA syAditi chenna | tasyA vinA.apyabhidhAnena lAbhAt.h | nahi lakShaNAdijij~nAsAmantareNa brahmajij~nAsA.asti | anyathA.anekaviShayatvena shAstrabhedaprasaN^gaH | nirviShayatAshaN^kApanodArthaM prayukttaM padamidaM karmAbhidhAnyeva yukttam.h | tadvijij~nAsasvetyAdishrutyarthAnugataM chaivaM sati sUtraM syAt.h |

tathA cha sarvAntaHpAtino vyavahArasataH pramANAdeH sAdhakatvasambhavAnnoktaprasaN^ga ityata Aha- vyavahArasatashcheti || chashabdo hetau | apishabdaH samuchchaye | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | vyavahArasato.api sAdhakatvaM pUrvasyAsata iva prativAdino na siddhameva yato.ato nokttaprasaN^ganistAra iti | ayamarthaH | yadi vyAvahArikaM sannAma sadeva tadA mithyAtvapratipAdanaM vyAhatam.h | phalitaM chAsmanmanorathadrumeNa | vyarthaM cha vyAvahArikapadam.h | atha tadasattadA kimanenAdhikamAcharitam.h | sattvAbhAve sAdhakatvaM na syAdityaniShyaprasaN^gasya tadavasthatvAditi | nanu cha dvividhaM sanmukhyamamukhyaM cha | tatra yasya sarvaprakAreNa bAdhitatvaM nAsti tanmukhyaM satpAramArthikamiti cha gIyate | yasya tu satpratItireva sattA tadamukhyaM sat.h | nacha tataH sattA siddhayati | tathAhi | kiM sattA.avagamamAtrAttatsattA.abhyupagamyeti manyase.abAdhitAttadavagamAdvA | nAdyaH | marumarIchikA.a.adau jalarUpatAsadbhAvAbhyupagamaprasaN^gAt.h | dvitIye.api vAdiprativAdimadhyasthamAsyi tasyApi kathAkAla eva bAdhitatvAvagamAbhAvAt.h | athavA kasyachidapi kAlAntare.api cha bAdhitatvabodhavirahAt.h | nAdyaH | atiprasaN^gAt.h | puruShatrayAvagatasyApyekakShaNAvagatasya puruShAntareNa tenApi kShaNAntare.api bahulaM bAdhadarshanAt.h | nachAsAvartho.asatyo.api dvitrAdipuuruShamAtrapUrvajAtatatpratItyanurodhAdbAdhadarshane saJNjAte.api tathaiva sannityabhyumabhyupagamyate | tasmAd.h dvitIyaH pakShaH parishiShyate | na chAsAvamukhye.astIti kutaH pAramArthyaprAptiH | nacha vAchyaM satpratIterapi pratItyantarameva sattetyanavastheti | pratIteH pAramArthikatvAt.h | nahi tasyA bAdho.asti | asti chetsaiva pratItirabAdhitA paramArthasatI | nacha pratIteH svarUpabhedo.astItyato vij~nAnaM brahmaiva paramArthasat.h | amukhyaM punardvedhA | mAyopAdhimavidyopAdhikaM cheti | tatrA.a.adyamambarAdikam.h | tachchAbrahmaj~nAnAdbAdhavaidhuryeNa hAnAdivyavahAranirvAhakatvAdvayAvahArikamiti gIyate | katipayapratipattR^ikatipayakAlatathAtvAvagamAdeva hi laukiko vyavahAraH pratIyate | dvitIyaM shukttirajatAdi | natu pratItisamayamAtraparivarti | na punarhAnAdiheturiti prAtitikamuchyate | tadevaM sattraividhyAdambarAdikaM vishvaM sadapi pAramArthikatvAbhAvAnmithyeti yujyate | vyAvahArikasattvAchcha tadantargatasya pramANA.a.adeH kathA.aN^gatopapadyate |  pAramArthikaprAtItikavyAvR^ittyarthatvena vyAvahArikapadaM cha sambhavatIti atredaM vakttavyam.h | kiM pAramArthikasadeva sadasachcha bAdhakabhedena dvividhamiti sattraividhyamuta satyevAntarabhedena | Adye prAgukttadoShanistAraH | nahi saditi j~nAnamAtreNAsadarthakriyArham.h | yena tathAvidhaM pramANAdi, kathAN^gatAM gachChet.h | tathAtve viShamapi pIyUShatayA.avagataM tadarthakriyAM kuryAt.h | bAdhavilambatArthakriyAkAritvaprasaN^gAt.h | yadapi tathaiva laukiko vyavahAraH pratIyata iti tadagre nirAkariShyate | arthakriyA.apyasatIti chetaretarAshrayAdinA nirastam.h | sato.arthakriyA.asambhavAdasatyeva kathaJNchitsA.aN^gIkAryeti chet.h | shrutiprAmANyanishchayottarakAlamevaitat.h | prAkttannishchayAtparamArthasata evArthakriyeti manyamAnaH prativAdI kathaM bodhanIyaH | anyonyAshrayAdiprasaN^gAdityukttam.h | 
dvitIyaM dUShayati- sattraividhyaM cheti || kenetyasya paramArthasatA vA vyAvahArikasatA vA prAtibhAsikasatA vA | Adye.api kimAtmetareNotA.a.atmanetyarthaH | pR^ichChyate.asmAbhiriti sheShaH | yathA asataH sAdhakatvasyeva tasya sattraividhyasyApi kathaJNchana vikalpitapakSheShu kasmiMshchana pakShe naiva siddhiH | kutaH | ukttaprakAreNaiva | tathA hi | na tAvatparamArthasattA.a.atmetareNa | dvaitA.a.apatteH | nApyAtmanaiva | tasya nirvisheShasya sAdhakatA.ayogAt.h | vyAvahArikaprAtItikayostu svarUpamevAdyApi na siddhamiti | nAmukhyaM sadasannapi sat.h | yenokttadoShaprasaN^gaH | kintvanirvachanIyam.h | nacha tadapi durvacham.h | sadasadvailakShaNyasyaiva tattvAt.h | tachchokttavidhayA vyAvahArikaprAtibhAsikabhedAd.h dvividham.h | tatra vyAvahArikasya prapaJNchasya sadasadvilakShasya sadvilakShaNatvAdupapannaM shrutyAdinA mithyAtvasamarthanam.h | asadvilakShaNatvAttadantargatasya pramANAdeH sAdhakatvaM cheti | syAdetadevaM kathaJNchidyadi vishvasya sadasadvilakShaNatvaM syAt.h | tadeva na siddhayatItyAha- vailakShaNyaM sadasatoriti || vishvasyeti sheShaH | sadasatoriti sambandhamAtre ShaShThI | tathAcha sadasadbhayAmityarthaH | etena | pramANavikalpanirAsena | tathAhi | vishvasya sadasadvailakShaNyaM kiM satA pramANena sAdhyate | utAsatA | atha sadasadvilakShaNena | nAdyaH | vAdino.anupapatteH | na dvitIyatR^itIyau | prativAdino.asampratipatteriti | nanvatra sadasadvailakShaNye sAdhakatvaM na syAditi prasaN^go vAchyaH | nacha tatra vyAptiH | maivam.h | sAkShiNi vyAptyavadhAraNopapatteH | sattvAbhAve sAdhakatvaM na syAditi vA prasaN^gaM vakShyAmaH | tatrAsattvamupAdhiriti chenna | tasya sattvAbhAvAnatirekAt.h | tadbhaN^gasya cha prAganirvachanIyasiddherashakyatvAt.h | etena sadvilakShaNatvAnmithyAtvopapAdanasadvilakShaNatvAtsAdhakatvaM chopapannamiti parAstam.h | sadvailakShaNye.asattvApattyA sAdhakatvAbhAvAsyAsadvailakShaNye cha sattvApAtena mithyAtvopapAdanasyAsambhavasyApatteH | prAganirvAchyasiddhervyAptidvayanirAsAyogAt.h | asadvailakShaNyamAtreNa hAnAdivyavahAropapattau shukttirajatAdAvapi tatprasaN^gaH | mAyA.avidyAvailakShaNyAnnaivamiti chenna | tasya nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | vailakShaNyamAtrasya prrakR^itAnupayogAditi | AstAM vA sattvAdivikalpanirAsena dUShaNAbhidhAnam.h | pramANameva prapaJNchAnirvachanIyatAyAM nopapadyate | nahi nehanAnetyAdishrutiH sadasadvailakShaNyalakShaNAnirvachanIyatAM vishvasya vaktti | 
atha manyeta | vivAdapadaM sadasadvilakShaNaM j~nAnabAdhyatvAdyadevaM tadevaM yathA shukttirajatamityanumAnaM vishvasya sadasadvilakShaNatve mAnam.h | tadbalAchChrutirapi tatraiva paryavasyatIti | tadasat.h | anumAnasyA.abhAsatvAdityAshayavAnprathamaprAptatvAtpratij~nAM tAvannirAkaroti- vailakShaNyaM satashcheti || chashabdAvavadhAraNe | apishabdau mithaH samuchchaye | ayamarthaH | kimatra sadasachChabdau bhAvAbhAvavAchinau | kiMvA vidyamAnAvidyamAnavAchinau | Adye dUShaNam.h | sato bhAvAtmakasya vishvasyAsato.abhAvAdvailakShaNyamapi bhAvAbhAvabhedavAdino mama mate svayaM sadastyeva | evamasato.abhAvAtmakasya vishvasya satA ebhAvAdvailakShaNyamapi bhedavAdinaH svayaM sadeva | atastena sAdhitena mamAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | kiM nAmaivaM vibhAgena sadasadvailakShaNyasiddhayA.api pratij~nAtArthasiddherarthAntaratA parasya syAditi || 1 || yadi cha pratyekaM bhAvAbhAvavailakShaNyaM vivakShitam.h 
| tadA sato bhAvasyApi vishvasya sato bhAvAdvailakShaNyaM bhAvabhedavAdino mama svayaM sadeva | bhAvAntaravailakShaNyAN^gIkArAt.h | asato.abhAvAdapi vailakShaNyaM sutarAM bhAvAbhAvabhedavAdinaH svayaM sadeva | evamasato.abhAvasya vishvasyAsato.abhAvAdvailakShaNyamabhAvabhedavAdinaH svayaM sadeva | abhAvAntaravailakShaNyAN^gIkArAt.h | sato bhAvAdvailakShaNyamapi sutarAM svayaM sadeveti tenAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h || 2 || 
bhAvAbhAvavailakShaNyaM nAma tattvAnadhikaraNatvaM vivakShitamiti chet.h | tathA.api sato bhAvasyApi vishvasyAsato.abhAvAdvailakShaNyamabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvamapi svayaM sadeva | asato.abhAvasya vishvasya sato bhAvAdvailakShaNyamapi bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvamapi mama svayaM sadeva | bhAvAbhAvabhedavAditvAt.h | yadi hi bhAve.apyabhAvatvamabhAve.api bhAvatvamaN^gIkuryAM kutastadA bhAvAbhAvabhedavAdaH | tathAcha kathaM tena sAdhyamAnenAniShyaM mama bhavet.h || 3 || atha pratyekaM bhAvAbhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM vivakShitamiti manyeta | tadA sato bhAvasyApi vishvasya bhAvAbhAvavailakShaNyaM bhAvAbhAvarUpatvAnadhikaraNatvaM mama svayaM sadeva | tathA.asato.abhAvasyApi vishvasyokttarUpaM vailakShaNyaM svayaM sadeva | bhAvabhAvabhedavAdinaikaikArthasyobhayarUpatA.anaN^gIkArAt.h | bhAve hi bhAvatvameva | nAbhAvatvamapi | abhAve chAbhAvatvameva | na bhAvatvamapItyatastena sAdhitenAniShyaM mama kathaM bhavet.h || 4 || athaikaikasya vastuno bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvamabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM cha sAdhyatayA vivakShitamiti manvIta | tathApi sato bhAvasyApi vishvasyAsato.abhAvAdvailakShaNyamabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM mama sadeva | evamasato.abhAvasyApi vishvasya sato bhAvAdvailakShaNyaM bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM svayaM sadeva | bhAvAbhAvabhedavAditvAt.h | ataH kathaM tenAniShyaM bhavet.h | aMshe siddhArthatayA parasya nigrahAt.h | ubhayasAdhanAdadoSha iti chenna | asiddhasannidhAne.api siddhasya tattvAnapAyAt.h | vishiShyasAdhanAnnaivamiti chenna | tathA.api vaiyarthyAnistArAt.h || 5 || 
atha bhAvAbhimate bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvamabhAvAbhimate chAbhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM sAdhyate | ato nokttadoSha iti chenna | tathA.api sato bhAvasyApi vishvasya sato vailakShaNyaM bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM mama svayaM sadeva | kathaM bhAvatvabhedavAdino naikameva bhAvatvaM sarvabhAveShvanugatam.h | kiM nAma pratibhAvaM bhAvatvAni bhidyante | pratipAdayiShyate chaitat.h | tathAcha bhAvo.api bhAvatvAntarAdhAro bhaviShyati | evamasato.abhAvarUpasyApi vishvasyAsato vailakShaNyamabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM mama svayaM sadeva | katham.h | abhAvatvabhedavAdinA.abhAve.apyabhAvatvAntarAbhAvasvIkArAt.h | tathA cha tenAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | parasyaiva siddhArthatA.anistArAt.h || 6 || atha bhAvAbhAvAbhimatayoH sarvathA bhAvAbhAvatve na sta ityartho vivakShitaH | tathA.api sata eva bhAvasyaivAsato vailakShaNyamabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM svayaM sadeva | yatastasmAdvishvasya tena sAdhitena bhedavAdino.aniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | idamukttaM bhavati | yadi prAgabhAvAdikaM pakShIkR^ityAbhAvatvAnadhikaraNamiti sAdhyate | tadA tasya bhAvatvaM pratij~nAtaM syAt.h | bhAvasyaivAbhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaniyamAt.h | dvau naJNau hi prakR^itamarthaM sAtishayaM gamayataH | evaM viyadAdikaM pakShIkR^itya bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatve sAdhyamAne tasyAbhAvatvaM pratij~nAtaM syAt.h | abhAvasyaiva bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaniyamAt.h | bhAvaniShedha eva hyabhAvaH | tathAcha vishvasya bhAvAbhAvavibhAgasya cha pareNAbhyupagatatvAnna bhAvAbhAvabhedavAdino mamAniShyaM kiJNchit.h | kintu bhAvAbhAvavyatikaramAtram.h | tatsAdhanaM cha prakR^itAnupayukttamiti || 7 || 
bhAvAbhAvAbhimatayorabhAvabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatve vAdiprativAdisaMmate bhAvAbhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvamapyadhikaM sAdhyate | ato nokttadoSha iti chenna | yataH sato bhAvasyaiva vishvasya viyadAderasato vailakShaNyamabhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM svayaM sadeva | pramitameva | yatashchAsato.abhAvasyaiva vishvasya prAgabhAvAdeH sato vailakShaNyaM bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM svayaM sadeva | pramitameva | yatashchAsato.abhAvasyaiva vishvasya prAgabhAvAdeH sato vailakShaNyaM bhAvatvAnadhikaraNatvaM svayaM sadeva | ato bhedavAdinastena viparItena pratij~nAtenAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | pratij~nAtArthasiddhau khalvaniShyaM bhavet.h | nahi pramANabAdhito.asau siddhayati | vyAvahArikabhAvatvAbhAvatvagocharaM pramANaM tattvaviShayeNAnumAnenaiva bAdhyata iti chenna | yato.asmAkaM tAvadbhAvAbhAvatvaviShayaM pramANaM tattvagocharameva | anyathA chakrakAdiprasaN^gAdatiprasaN^gAchcheti || 8 || dvitIye.apyetadevottaram.h | vishvasya sataH satyAdvailakShaNyamapi mama svayaM svamatameva | tathA.asato.avidyamAnAdapi vailakShaNyaM svayameva | atastena sAdhitena mamAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | bhavatu vishvasyAtmanaH shashaviShANAdervailakShaNyaM svamatam.h | sato vailakShaNyaM tu katham.h | sattvAN^gIkArAditi chenmaivam.h | sato vidyamAnasyApyasato bhedaM vadato mama yathA vishvasyAsato vailakShaNyaM svayameva | tathA sato.api vishvasya sato vailakShaNyaM satAM bhedavAdinaH svayameva | sadantaravailakShaNyAt.h || 9 || sattvAsattvAnadhikaraNatvaM sadasadvilakShaNatvamiti chet.h | tadA.api sato vishvasyAsato vailakShaNyaM sadasadbhedavAdinaH svayaM sadeva | atastena sAdhitena mamAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | parasyaivAMshataH siddhArthatA bhavet.h | tarhi sattvAnAdhAratvameva sAdhyata iti chenna | asata eva hi sato vailakShaNyaM sattvAnadhikaraNatvaM bhedavAdino mama svayaM sadeva niyamena bhavati | tathAcha vishvasya tena sattvAnadhikaraNatvena sAdhitenAsattvApattyA parasyaivAniShyaM bhavet.h | aniShyaprasaN^gena paraM nigR^ihItavato mamAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h || 10 || 
athAsattvAnadhikaraNatve vAdiprativAdisiddhe sattvAnadhikaraNatvamapyadhikaM sAdhyata iti chenna | aniShyAnistArAt.h | kiJNcha, na sattvaM nAmaikamanugataM kintu prativastu sattvAni bhidyante | tatra viyadAderasadvailakShaNye sati sattvAnadhikaraNatvaM sAdhyamAnaM kimekasattvAnadhikaraNatvamutAnekasattvAnadhikaraNatvamatha sarvasattvAnadhikaraNatvam.h | kiM vA.avisheShitasattvAnadhikaraNatvam.h | athavA sarvathA sattvAnadhikaraNatvaM vivakShitam.h | nAdyaH | vishvasyAsato.api vailakShaNyaM tAvanmama svayameva sato.api vailakShaNyaM sattvAnadhikaraNatvamapi svayameva | katham.h | sattvabhedavAdino mama sato.api sattvAntarAnadhikaraNatvAN^gIkArAt.h | tathAcha siddhena tena sAdhyamAnena mamAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | evameva chaturthanirAkaraNamapi vyAkhyeyam.h | na dvitIyatR^itIyau | vishvasyAsato vailakShaNyamasattvAnadhikaraNatvaM tAvanmama svayameva | sato vailakShaNyamanekasattvAnadhikaraNatvam.h | sarvasattvAnadhikaraNatvaM tAvanmama svayameva | sato vailakShaNyamanekasattvAnadhikaraNatvam.h | 
sarvasattvAnadhikaraNatvamapi svayaM sadeva | katham.h | bhedavAdinaikaikasyArthasyAnekasarvasattvAsvIkArAt.h | svIkAre cha bhedabhaN^gaH syAt.h | tatashcha tenAniShyaM kathaM bhavet.h | na paJNchamaH | yataH sata evAsato vailakShaNyaM svayaM tadeva | niyatamevAsti | yatashchAsata eva sato vailakShaNyamapi niyatamevAtastena sAdhyamAnena vishvasya sadasattvApattyA bhedavAdinaH kathamaniShyaM bhavet.h | mayA hyekasyaiva sadasattvamaN^gIkR^itam.h | svopAdhau pratiShedhApratiyogitvAtparopAdhau cha tatpratiyogitvAt.h | dvayorapi sarvathA pratiShedhAtkathaM sadasattvaprasaN^ga iti chettarhyasata eva sato vailakShaNyaM svayaM sanniyatameva | ataH sadvailakShaNyamuktavA punarasato.api vailakShaNyena vyAhatena pratij~nAtena bhedavAdinaH kathamaniShyaM bhavet.h | evaM sata evAsato.api vailakShaNyaM niyatamityasadvailakShaNyamuktavA punarvishvasya sadvailakShaNyapratij~nA vyAhatA draShyavyA | nahyanirvAchyasiddheH prAgayaM vipratiShedho nivArayituM shakyaH | asmAdeva hetostatsiddhiriti chettarhi mAtA vandhyeti pratij~nA kuto vipratiShiddhA | vakShyamANahetunaiva pratij~nAtArthasiddhestatrApi suvachatvAt.h | "sambhAvitaH pratij~nAyA arthaH sAdhyeta hetunA' iti nyAyAttatra hetvAkAN^kShaiva nAstIti chetsatyam.h | kiJNcha sata eva vishvasyAsato vailakShaNyaM svayaM sadeva | sAkShipramitamasti | atastena bAdhitena sarvathA sattvAnadhikaraNatvena pratij~nAtena bhedavAdinaH kathamaniShyaM bhavet.h | amukhyasattvAvedakaM pramANaM taditi chet.h | mama tAvanmukhyameva tatsatvamityukttam.h | parakIyapramANatarkANAmadyApi gahane niviShyatvAditi | kechitte tavAniShyaM kataM na bhavediti vyAchakShate | tatra na pAdAdAviti pratiShedhasya naJNA nirdiShyamanityamiti samAdhAnamavaseyam.h | 
dvitIye dUShaNAntaramAha- yadyuchyata iti || apishabdo dUShaNasamuchchaye | sarvasmAdapItyabhividhau vA | yadIti shravaNAttarhIti grAhyam.h | sarvashabdo.anekArthaH | yadyanekasmAtsato vailakShaNyAt.h | anekasattvAnadhikaraNatvaM vishvasya sAdhyamityuchyate tarhi satAM bhedasaMsthitistatashchApasiddhAntaH | idamukttaM bhavati | vishvamanekasattA.anadhikaraNamiti pratijAnatA.anekasattvAnyaN^gIkriyante na vA | dvitIye.anekavisheShaNaM vyatharm.h | Adye.apyekasminnevArthe.anekAni sattvAnyutAdhArabhedena | nAdyaH | vaiyarthyAt.h | dvitIye tvidamupatiShThate | sadbhedasaMsthitiriti | anekasattvAdhikaraNatApratiShedhasAmarthyAdekaikasattvasvIkArApatteriti vA | tR^itIyasya vedaM dUShaNAntaram.h | yadi sarvasmAtsato vailakShaNyaM sarvasattvAnadhikaraNatvaM vishvasya sAdhyatayochyate tarhi sadbhedasaMsthitiH | na hyanekasadanaN^gIkAre sarvashabdasya prayAjenamasti | santyevAnekAni santi pAramAthirkaM tvekameveti chenna | tatsiddhayarthamevAdyApi bhavatA prayatanAt.h | tadanadhikaraNatvasAdhaneM.ashe.apasiddhAntAt.h | chatuthare dUShaNAntaramAha- sanmAtratvamiti || avivakShitavisheShaM sattvaM yasmAdbrahmaNo.apyasti | tasmAtkAraNAttasmAtsato brahmaNastadvailakShaNyam.h | tatsattvAnadhikaraNatvamapi vishvasya no.asmAkaM mataM bhavet.h | tathAcha siddhatvAttadapi sAdhyaM no bhavet.h | avivakShitavisheShasattvAnadhikaraNatve sAdhye brahmagatasattvAnadhikaraNatayA.api pratij~nAtArthopapatterarthAntarateti | 
athavA kimidaM sattvaM nAma | yadanadhikaraNatvaM vishvasya sAdhyate | kiM sAmAnyasattvamuta svarUpasattvam.h | AdyaM dUShayati- yadyuchyata iti || sarvasmAtsarvArthAnugatAtsAmAnyAdvailakShaNyaM tadanAdhAratvamiti yAvat.h | sAdhyatayA yadyuchyate tadA sadbhedasaMsthitiH | yadi sattaiva nAsti tadA tadanadhikaraNatvapratij~nA vyArthA syAt.h | nedaM shashaviShANAdhikaraNamitivadvipratipatterevAnudayAt.h | sattAsAmAnyAN^gIkAre cha sadbhedo durvAra eva | na hyekAshrayaM sAmAnyamasti | santi sattAdhikaraNAni santIti chettarhi kAnIti vakttavyAni | evaM pratij~nAM nirAkR^itya hetumapyapAkaroti- j~nAnabAdhyatvamiti || na kevalaM pratij~nA duShyA | kiM nAma hetubhUtaM j~nAnabAdhyatvamapItyarthaH | tushabdaH siddhAntyabhimatAjj~nAnabAdhyatvAdvayavachChinatti | j~nAnabAdhyatvaM hi j~nAnanivartyatvaM vA pratipannopAdhau niShedhapratiyogitvaM vA hetutvena parasyAbhimatam.h | nacha prapaJNche tatprativAdino mama siddham.h | ato.anyatarAsiddho heturiti | nanvIshvaraj~nAnena prapaJNchanivR^ittistvayA.apIShyata eva | anyathA tasya saMhArakartR^itvAnupapatteH | j~nAnAdimata eva katarR^itvAt.h | satyam.h | naivaM j~nAnanivartyatvaM parasyAbhipretam.h | api tarhyaj~nAnopAdAnakasya samAne viShaye virodhitA j~nAnenopAdAne nivR^itte svayameva vilapanam.h | yathA.a.aha | "aj~nAnasya svakAryeNa vartamAnena pravilInena vA saha j~nAnena nivR^ittibAdhaH' iti | na chAyaM prapaJNche.asmAkaM saMmataH | kintu mudgaraprahArAdinA ghaTasyeveshvarasya j~nAnechChAprayatnavyApArairvinAsha eva | sa eva heturastviti chenna | tathAvidhamapi j~nAnabAdhyatvaM pakShaikadeshe prakR^ityAdau na siddhaM prativAdina iti bhAgAsiddhatvAt.h | kiJNcha satyasyApi j~nAnavinAshyatvamastu | nacha vipakShe kiJNchidbAdhakamastItyato.aprayojakatvAjj~nAnabAdhyatvaM na siddhamapi vyApyatvAsiddhamapIti yAvat.h | prativAdino mateneti guDajihvikAmAtram.h | bAdhakAnupanyAse vAdino.api vyApyatvAsiddherAvashyakatvAt.h | sato vinAshe chaitanyasyiApa vinAshaprasaN^ga iti chet.h 
| tarhi vinAshamAtrasya sAdhyaprayojakatvena j~nAnabAdhyatvamasiddhamapi | vyarthavisheShaNAsiddhamapi syAt.h | nAshyatvamAtraM heturj~nAneti svarUpakathanamAtram.h | sa chokttabAdhakasAnAthyena nAprayojaka iti chenna | sattvasAmye.api vinAshakAraNasadasadbhAvena visheShasyokttatvAt.h | nanu cha nehanAnA.astItipratipannopAdhau shrautaniShedhAtmA bAdhaH prapaJNche.astIti chenna | shrutyarthanirNayottarakAlamevaitat.h | sa eva tUpapattivirodhAdashakya ityuchyamAnatvAt.h | athavA j~nAnabAdhyatvamasiddhaM vyAptirahitamapIti yojyam.h | tathA hi | kiM tvadabhimataM j~nAnabAdhyatvamatra hetUkriyate kiM vA.asmadabhimatamiti vAchyam.h | AdyaM chedukttanyAyena na siddhaM prativAdinaH | dvitIye vyAptivaidhuryamiti | tatkathamityata Aha- vij~nAtasyeti || hi yasmAdanyathAvij~nAtasya samyagvij~nAnameva bAdhastadviShayatvameva tadbAdhyatvaM matamasmAkam.h | tachchAtmani vipakShe gatamiti vyAptivikalamiti vAkyasheShaH | satyo.apyAtmA dehAdyAtmanA vij~nAto vedAntajanitasamyagvij~nAnavR^ittiviShaya iti pareNApyaN^gIkAryam.h | anyathA avidyAnivR^ittyanupapatteriti |

| nirAkariShyate chAsau durvichArastatra tatreti | dvitIyamapi lakShaNaM nirAkaroti- j~nAnabAdhyatvamiti || yadi j~nAnabAdhyatvaM nAmokttavidhayA shukttirajatAdeshchAsatvenAvidyopAdAnakatvAbhAvAt.h | kimapyaN^gIkaraNIyameva | padasya nirarthakatvAyogAt.h | tadevAsmAkamanirvachanIyalakShaNaM bhavatvityata Aha- prativAdino vij~nAtasyeti || prativAdino mama matamiti sambandhaH | tachchAtmanyanirvachanIye.apyastItyativyAptamiti sheShaH | atrAnyathAvij~nAnameva bhrAntiH | tatprasaJNjitAnyathA.a.akAraloDanaM samyagvij~nAnameva bAdha ityavadhAraNatayA matAntarANi nirastAni veditavyAni | hi shabdena tatra pramANaprasiddhiM sUchayati | 
atha paJNchAkhyAtivAdaH || iha khalu kechidyathArthameva sarvavij~nAnamiti manyamAnA nAnyathAkhyAtiM sahante | tathA hi | keyamanyathAkhyAtirnAma | yadi tAvadanyathApariNate vastuni khyAtiranyathAkhyAtiH | tadA ghaTAdipratyayAH sarve.apyanyathAkhyAtitvAdvibhramAH prasajyeran.h | kiJNcha shukttikAyA rajatAkArapariNAmaH kiM sakAraNa utAkAraNaH | na tAvadakAraNaH | kAdAchitkatvAnupapatteH | Adye kAraNaM vAchyam.h | karaNadoSha iti chenna | tasya karaNasambandhinaH shukttikApariNAmahetutvAnupapatteH | anyathA tadaiva sakalArthAnAM rajatarUpapariNAmaprasaN^gAt.h | duShyakaraNasaMsargo heturiti chettathApi kiM shukttitvApagamena rajatarUpapariNAmaH | kiM vA tadanapagamena | Adye puruShAntareNApi tadA shukttitvaM na pratyetavyam | dvitIye bhrAntenApi tatpratyetavyam.h | kiJNcha shukttitvApagame bAdhe.api na tadbhay.hA | atha punaH shuktayAkAreNa rajataM pariNatamiti chenna | karaNadoShasya kAraNasyAbhAvAt.h | bAdho.apyevaM tenaiva gR^ihyata iti chenna | ghaTAderapi kulAlAdimAtravedyatApAtAt.h | sukhAdivaditi chenna | bAhyAntaratvena visheShAt.h | anyathokttAtiprasaN^gAnistArAt.h | 
kiJNcha doShavashAdrajatAkAreNa pariNatA chechChukttistadA doShApagame.api tathaiva kathaM nAvatiShThate | nahi nimittakAraNanAshAtkAryanAsho dR^iShyaH | kamalakuD.hmalavikAsanimittasAvitratejo.apagamasya vikAsanivR^ittihetutA dR^iShyeti chenmaivam.h | dalavibhAgo hi vikAso nAma | sa cha kShaNikatvAtsatyeva sAvitratejasi nivR^ittaH | saMyogapradhvaMsastu na kadA.api nivartate punaH saMyogalakShaNo mukulIbhAvastu shItAdinodanajanya eva | sthAyitve.api vibhAgasyAnyadeva tannAshe nimittamiti yatkiJNchidetat.h | paratvAdivatsyAditi chenna | vipratipatteH | kiJNchotpannaM chedrajataM vinaShyaM tadA tathaiva pratItiH syAt.h na punarnedaM rajatamiti bAdhabuddhiH | etena duShyakaraNajanyAdvij~nAnAdrajatametyapi parAstam.h | kA chaivaM sati doShavAchoyukttiH | nahi mR^ido ghaTAkArapariNAmasya nimittaM daNDachakrAdikaM doShatvena manyante | kiJNcha yasyAH pratItestadAlambanaM tata eva tajjanma  kiMvA pratItyantarAt.h | nAdyaH | parasparAshrayaprasaN^gAt.h | utpanne hi rajate tadAlambanAyAH pratIterjanma, tasyAM jAtAyAM rajatotpattiriti | na khalu nirAlambanA pratItirutpadyate | dvitIye.api kiM tatpratItyantaraM shukttikA.a.alambanam.h | uta shukttikArajatAntarAlambanam.h | athavA.atharAntarAlambanam.h | nAdyaH | sarvatra shukttipratItyanantaraM rajatotpAdaprasaN^gAt.h | shukttirajatapratIteH prAk.h shukttiriti pratItiniyamAbhAvAchcha | duShyakaraNAlochitashukttisAdhAraNAkArapratIte rajatajanmeti chenna | sAdhAraNAkAramAtradarshanAnantaraM rajatapratItiniyamAbhAvAt.h | kAraNavaikalyaM tatra kalpyata iti chet.h | syAdetadevam.h | yadi rajatajanma pramitaM syAt.h | pratItiM tu prakArAntareNopapAdayiShyAmaH | na dvitIyaH | pUrvarajatasyApi tadeva kAraNamiti rajatapratItipravAhAvichChedaprasaN^gAt.h | na tR^itIyaH | atiprasaN^gAt.h | tadevaM bhrAntibAdhayoranupapatterna pariNAmapakSho yukttaH | 
nApi vastuno vastvantarAtmanA.avabhAso.anyathAkhyAtiriti yukttam.h | tathA hi kiM vastuno vastvantarAtmanA satI utAsatI | Adye na bhrAntirnApi bAdhaH | sarveShAM cha sarvaM sarvAtmanA pratIyeta | na hi doShaH karaNasaMskAraH | tathA satyaduShyakAraNena na kiJNchidupalabhyeta | kiJNchaivaM sati rajatasaMvitsamIchInA shukttireveyamiti chAsamIchInetyApadyeta | na dvitIyaH | asataH pratItyanupapatteH | upapattau vA kiM rajatasyApi vastutvagrahaNena | etenAsambaddhavisheShaNavishiShyapratItiranyathAkhyAtiriti nirastam.h | asato visheShaNasambandhasya pratItyanupapatteH | upapattau vA kimasatkhyAtivAdibhiraparArddham.h | atha brUShe.anyAkAraM j~nAnamanyathAkhyAtiriti | tadasat.h | samIchInaj~nAnasyApyAntarabAhyatvAdinA.arthavilakShaNAkAratvena vibhramatvApatteH | anyAkArollekhij~nAnamanyAlambanamanyathAkhyAtiriti tu viruddham.h | tathA hi | na tAvatsadasadbhAvamAtreNAlambanaM sadbhAvamAtrasya sarvavastupratyayasAdhAraNyena sarvapratyayAnAM sarvArthAlambanatvApatteH | sarvaM sarvaj~natA chaivaM sati syAt.h | atItAdiviShayasya nirAlambanatApAtashcha | etena purodeshe sadbhAvenAlambanatvamapi pratyukttam.h | nacha kAraNatvenAlambanam.h | rUpAdij~nAnasya chakShurAdyapi kAraNamiti tadAlambanatvaprasaN^gAt.h | atItAnAgataviShayatvaM cha j~nAnasya na syAt.h | atItAnAgatayorasattvena kAraNatvAnupapatteH | etena viShayatayA kAraNatvamityapi nirastam.h | AtmAshrayatvaM chaivaM sati syAt.h | viShayatvasyaiva nirUpyamANatvAt.h | kiJNchaivaM viShayatvamityevAstu | kiM kAraNatayA vyarthayA.anarthajananyA | kiM chedaM viShayatvam.h | yena yasyAtishaya utpadyate sa tasya viShaya iti chet.h | atishayo hi j~nAtatA vA syAdvayavahAro vA | nAdyaH | anabhyupagamAt.h | abhyupagame.apyatItAdij~nAnasya nirviShayatvApAtAt.h | na hyasati dharmiNi dharmotpAdo yujyate | na dvitIyaH | atadarthino vyavahArAnutpattAvaviShayatvApatteH | vyAghrachorAdij~nAnAnantaramAdIyamAnasya daNDAderapi tadviShayatvaprasaktteshcha | yadvij~nAnaM yadAkAraM tattadAlambanamiti tu tathAgatamatamanudhAvati | 
yatsannikR^iShyakaraNena yajj~nAnaM janyate tattadviShayamityapi na | rUpAdij~nAnasyAkAshAdiviShayatApAtAt.h | nahi rUpAdij~nAnamutpAdayachchakShurAkAshAdinA na sannikR^iShyata iti yujyate | pratyabhij~nA cha tattA.asannikR^iShyakaraNajanyA na tadviShayA syAt.h | nacha vAkyaM vAkyArthena sannikR^iShyate | yena tajjanitaj~nAnasya vAkyArtho viShayaH sy.hA | AkAshAdiviShayataivaM chApadyeta | liN^gaj~nAnAchchAtmasannikR^iShyAjjAyamAnaM liN^gij~nAnamAtmaviShayamApadyeta | tasmAdyajj~nAnaM yatpratibhAsaM tadeva tasyAlambanamiti mantavyam | tatra rajataj~nAne shukttiravabhAsate na veti vakttavyam.h | avabhAsata iti bruvANaH shlAghanIyapraj~no devAnAM priyaH | yadi saMvidi bahumAnavAnneti brUyAttadA kathaM tachChukttikAlambanaM syAt.h | kiJNcha rajatamavabhAsate shukttikAlambanaM chedatiprasaN^gaH kataM pariharaNIyaH | nanu rajatAvabhAsasya rajataviShayakatve tena rajatena bhavitavyam.h | kathaM na bhavitavyam.h | nahi sampratipannasamIchInarajatasvIkAre.api nimittamastyanyadrajatAvabhAsAt.h | na hyanyatararajatapratibhAsapakShapAte kAraNamasti | nAstyatra rajatamityapi 
pratibhAso.astIti chet.h | satyam.h | pratibhAsasAmarthyAdrajatAbhAvo.apyaN^gIkR^ita eva purataH | pratItyorvirodhaH syAditi chenna | yathA na virodhastathA vakShyamANatvAt.h |

kuNDalI devadatta ityasyApi j~nAnasya daNDakuNDaladevadattatvatAdAtmyaviShayatApAtAt.h | tR^itIyastu syAdeva | samAnamekamadhikaraNaM yeShAM te hi samAnAdhikaraNAsteShAM bhAvaH sAmAnAdhikaraNyam.h | tathAcha guNAdInAmAshrayeNa parasparaM cha bhedaH AshrayANAM chAbhedaH sphuTa eva | nahi svayameva svasyAdhikaraNam.h | nApi samAnamadhikaraNaM yeShAmiti parasparAbhede yujyate | nachAshrayabhede tasya samAnatA.asti | nacha guNAdyAshrayasya bhede pramANamasti | vishiShyayorbhede.api na tat.h guNAdyAshrayaH | kintu guNAdyAshrayAshritaM vastvantaraM tat.h | evaJNcha yatra bhedo na tadabhedena pratibhAsate yachchAbhedena prachibhAsate na tatra bheda iti kvAtivyAptiH | nanu guNAdInAmAshrayeNa parasparaM chAbhedo bhagavato muneH siddhAntaH | kvachidbhedAbhedau cha | sAmAnAdhikaraNyapratItistu bhedaniShThaiva vyAkhyAtA | tathAcha punaH shuklaH paTa ityAdipratyayA vibhramAH prasakttAH | maivam.h | savisheShatvAN^gIvakArAt.h | vishadaM chaitadvisheShanirUpaNe vyutpAdayiShyAmaH |
yatpunaranyAkArollekhItyAdinA.asmadabhimatAnyathAkhyAteranubhavavirodhaM pratij~nAya tadupapAdanAya yatsannikR^iShyakaraNenetyantenAlambanalakShaNanirAkaraNaM kR^itaM tadanumatamevAsmAkam.h | yadvij~nAnaM yatsannikR^iShyakaraNena janyate sa tasya viShaya ityaN^gIkArAt.h | nanvatrApi doSho.abhihita iti chenna | sannikarShasyApi kAraNatayA vivakShitatvena tasyAsambaddhatvAt.h | nahi chakShurAderAkAshAdisannikarSho rUpAdij~nAnakAraNam.h, nApi vAkyasyAkAshAdisannikarSho vAkyArthaj~nAne hetuH, nacha liN^gaj~nAnasyAtmanA sannikarSho liN^gij~nAnanimittam.h, kiM nAmAvarjanIyasannidhayaste sannikarShAH | liN^gasya sAdhyadharmisannikarSho liN^gij~nAnakAraNamiti chenna liN^gaj~nAnasya karaNatayA.abhyupagamAt.h | anenaiva vAkyasya shrotR^ishrotrasannikarShAshrayaNena dUShaNaM parAstam.h | vAkyaj~nAnasyaiva karaNatvAN^gIkArAt.h | tathA.api pratyabhij~nAyAM tattAMshena chakShurAderliN^ginA cha liN^gaj~nAnasya vAkyArthena vAkyaj~nAnasya sannikarShAbhAvAdaviShayatApattiriti chenna asannikR^iShyaj~nApane.atiprasaN^gAt.h | tadanubhavajanitasaMskArasahakR^itendriyeNa pratyabhij~nA jAyate, tadvayAptaliN^gaviShayeNa cha liN^gaj~nAnena liN^gij~nAnamutpadyate, saMsargadharmakapadArthavAchipadasamudAyarUpavAkyaviShayaj~nAnena vAkyArthaj~nAnaM janyate, ato nAtiprasaN^ga iti chettarhyabhyupagataH sannikarShaH | nahi saMyogAdireva sannikarShaH kiM nAma pratyAsattimAtram.h |

aiathaivaM manyeta | astyeva vyavaharturanvayaj~nAnam.h | kiM nAma sadapi na pravR^ittAvupayujyate | ato na kashchiddoSha iti | tatra kiM tadanvayaj~nAnaM pravR^ittau niyatamutAniyatamiti vAchyam.h | Adye.astu tatpravR^ittAvupayogi mA vA bhUt.h, anyathAkhyAtiM vinA na rajatArthinaH purovartini pravR^ittiriti tAvatsiddham.h | dvitIye tu shabdochChedastadavasthaH | kiJNcha niyatapUrvabhAvi chAkAraNaM chetyanupapannam.h | pratibhAsamAnayorasaMsargAgrahe sati saMsargagraho.avarjanIyasannidhiriti chenna viparyayasyApi vakttuM shakyatvAt.h | avashyaM chaitadevam.h | vyavahAro hi vyavahartavyopalambhanibandhano yukttaH, na tu vyavaharaNIyaviparyayAnupalabdhinibandhanaH | nahi ghaTavyavahAro vyavahartavyaj~nAnapuraHsaro vyavahAratvAdghaTavyavahAravat.h | vivAdapadaM j~nAnaM purovartiviShayaM tadviShayavyavahArajanakatvAtsaMmatavat.h | purovarti vA rajataj~nAnagocharo rajataj~nAnagocharo rajatAnupAyatve sati tadarthipravR^ittiviShayatvAtsamyagrajatavat.h | vivAdapadaM rajataj~nAnamidaM j~nAnAnna bhidyate prakAshamAnAttato.aprakAshamAnabhedatve sati prakAshamAnatvAtsampratipannarajataj~nAnavadityAdayaH | kiJNcha viparyayAbhAve nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnasya bAdhakatvamanupapadyamAnaM taM gamayati | nahi tathAtve bAdhakatvamasti | na tAvadagrahaNanivartakatayA bAdhakatvam.h, sarvapratyayAnAM tathAtvApAtAt.h | nApi vyavahAravichChedakatvena, atadarthinAM vyavahArAnutpattau nedaM rajatamitij~nAnasyAbAdhakatvaprasaN^gAt.h, vyAghrachorAdij~nAnasyApi pravR^ittivichChedakatvena bAdhakatvaprasaktteshcha | nachArthasya vyavahArayogyatAvichChedakatvena, samayAntare.api tatra vibhramAtpravR^ittyabhAvApatteH | nacha vyavahArapratibandhakatvena, avivekanivR^ittau kAraNAbhAvAdeva 
vyavahArAnupapatteH pratibandhakakalpanAyogAt.h, vyAghrachorAdij~nAnasya bAdhakatApatteshcha | vimatamayathArthaM bAdhyatvAdvayavahAravaditi | ata eva bhrAntitvaprasiddhayApi viparyAsasiddhiH | evaMcha sati pratyayatvAnumAnaM kAlAtyayApadiShyaM veditavyam.h | aduShyakaraNajanyatvopAdhigrastaM cha | etena rajataj~nAnatvAnumAnamapi nirastam.h | anyathA vimato vyavahAro yathArtho vyavahAratvAt.h, rajataviShayo vA rajatavyavahAratvAdityapi syAt.h | 
yadapi j~nAnatvaM cha yathArthamAtravR^ittItyAdi, tatra kimidaM j~nAnatvaM sAmAnyaM vA pratiniyataM vA | nAdyaH | vAdiprativAdinorAshrayAsiddheH | dvitIye yathArthaj~nAnavR^ittij~nAnatve siddhasAdhanatA | vimataj~nAnavR^ittij~nAnatvapakShIkAre.api mAtreti vyarthaM syAt.h | tattyAgena cha pratij~nAne prathamAnumAnadoSha eva | kiJNcha yathAtharmAtravR^ittItyayathArthAvR^ittitvamAtraM vivakShitam.h utAyathAtharj~nAnAvR^ittitvam.h | Adye siddhasAdhanam.h ayathArthavyavahArAvR^ittitvasya siddhatvAt.h | dvitIye parasyAprasiddhavisheShaNatA, aduShTasAmagrIjanyamAtravR^ittitvamapAdhishcha | yachcha shukttikA rajatatvenAbhAsata ityAdi, tadapyasat.h | meruH sarShapa ityAdivAyAnmerorapi sarShapatvena pratibhAsAd.hdR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavaikalyAt.h | anyathA tathAvidhavAkyAbhAsaM shrutavatA tatpratiShedho na kriyetAprasakttatvAt.h | nahi padArthapratiShedho yukttaH | api chaivaM satyagniranuguNa iti bAdhitaviShayasya vAkyasya ghaTaH pachatItyapArthakAdbhedo na syAt.h | yadapIdaM rajatatAdAtmyamityAdi | tachchAyukttam.h | tadapratItAvAshrayAsiddheH, pratItau vyAghAtAt.h dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyasamatvAchchetyAstAM vistaraH || 1 || 
kashchitpunarevamAha | tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itamekaikAmakarodityAdishruteH, sametyAnyonyasaMyogamityAdipurANAt.h, tyAtmakatvAdisUtrAchcha anyathA shvetaketUddAlakAkhyAyikayA pratipAditatvAdadvaitamapi na shrutyabhiprAyaH syAt.h | "taddhaitatpashyan.h R^iShirvAmadevaH pratipedehaM brahmAsmi' ityapi paropAsanAnuvAdo na svArthe tAtparyavAn.h syAt.h "atha yo.anyAM devatAmupAste' itayupAsanAprakaraNatvAt.h | tathAcha bahuviplavaH syAt.h | tasmAtsUtrakArasyaivAyamabhiprAyo yajjagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM brahmaNaH svarUpAntargatameva lakShaNamiti | tathAcha vispaShyatadIyavAkyAntarabalAdasyApi sUtrasya svarUpalakShaNaparatvameveti | 
yata evaM jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM svalakShaNamatra sUtre brahmaNo.abhidhIyate, tato na paramate.asya sUtrasyArambha evopapadyate | ityAha- ata iti || 
lakShaNaM hi sajAtIyavijAtIyavyavachChedArthaM bhavati | yathA.a.aha "samAnAsamAnajAtIyavyavachChedo vA lakShaNArthaH' iti | tathAchAnena lakShaNena sajAtIyAjjIvAdvijAtIyAjjaDAchcha brahmavyAvartitaM sUtrakAreNa | jIvaikyanirAkaraNasUtrasyArambhaH kathaM jIvaikyavAdinAM syAt.h | syAdyadIdaM kathaJNchit.h (syAtkathaJNchidyadIdaM) taTasthalakShaNaM syAt.h | svarUpalakShaNamiti chopapAditam.h | 
syAdayamadvaitinAmanupapanno lakShaNArambho yadIdaM jIvavyAvR^ittyarthaM lakShaNamukttaM syAt.h | jaDamAtravyAvR^ittyarthaM tu lakShaNe vyAkhyAyamAne kathaM jIvaikyavAdinAM lakShaNasUtrArambho.anupapanna ityata Aha- nahIti ||
yatra hi lakShaNaM nAsti tatsarvaM tadvayAvartyamaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | anyathA lakShaNasyAvyAptiprasaN^gAt.h | nachedaM lakShaNaM jIvasyAsti | tatkathamasAvanena na vyAvartyata iti |
kiJNchAnena lakShaNena yadi jIvo na vyAvartyate, kintu so.api lakShyAntargataH | tathA sati lakShaNasya jIve.ativyAptimAshaN^kayetaravyapadeshAddhitAkaraNAdidoShaprasakttiriti sUtrakArIyaM tannirAkaraNamasaN^gataM syAt.h | nahi lakShya evAtivyAptirlakShaNasya kenApi shaN^kayate | kathaJNchichChaN^kAyAM vA tasyApi lakShyatvAN^gIkAraM parityajya tatra na lakShaNanirAkaraNaM kriyata ityAshavAnAha- hitAkriyeti || 
yadyapi pareNApi jIvasya lakShaNavyAvartyatvamaN^gIkR^itameva, yathA.a.aha "sarvaj~naM sarvashakttiM vihAyAnyataH paraparikalpitAtpradhAnAderachetanAchchetanAdapi parichChinnaj~nAnakriyAshaktteH saMsAriNo hiraNyagarbhAdutpattyAdi na sambhAvayitumapi shakyate' iti, tathA.api nyAyenopapAdayitumidamukttamiti | 
ito.api mAyAvAdinAM na brahmalakShaNasUtrArambhaH sambhavatItyAha- nirguNatvaM cheti || 
lakShaNavAkyaM hi sAkShAllakShyasyAsAdhAraNadharmasaMsargaM pratipAdayadarthAditaravyAvR^ittiM pratipAdayati | tato.anenApi lakShaNAvAkyena brahmaNo jagajjanmAdikAraNatvena tadavinAbhUtaiH sarvaj~natvAdibhishcha saMsargaH pratipAdanIyaH | tathAcha nirvisheShatvaM brahmaNo.anena sUtreNa niShiddham.h | nirvisheShatvavAdinAM cha nirvisheShatvaM niShedhataH sUtrasyArambhaH kathamupapadyata iti |
syAdiyaM jIvabrahmaNorekatvaM brahmaNashcha nirguNatvamaN^gIkurvatAM lakShaNasUtrArambhAnupapattiH | yadyanena sUtreNa jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM brahmaNaH svalakShaNamuchyate | na chaivaM kintu taTasthameva | nahi tathAvidhaM jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM jIvabrahmaNorekatvaM vA brahmaNo nirguNatvaM vA viruNaddhi | 
nanu svalakShaNatve pramANamukttam.h | maivam.h | svasya lakShaNAni svalakShaNAnIti vA | su samyak.h svarUpAntargatyA na lakShaNAnIti vA tadarthopapatteH | tarhi yato.asya janmAdi sA mAyA tadAshrayo brahmeti nirdeshaH syAt.h | natu janmAdyasya yatastadbrahmeti | maivam.h | yatra ghoShaH sA gaN^getivallakShaNayA prayogopapatteH | nanu taTasthenApi jagajjanmAdikAraNatvena brahmaNo jIvaikyaM nirguNatvaM cha (ni)viruddhayate | kAkanilayanatvaM hi pareNa taTasthaM lakShaNamudAhR^itam.h | tasya lakShyAntarbhAve kAkAdhikaraNatvamapi gR^ihashabdAtharH syAt.h | tatashcha kAkavigame gR^ihaikadeshabhaN^gabuddhiH syAt.h iti | tatra kAkAdhikaraNatvaM tadanadhikaraNebhyo gR^ihaM vyAvartayati na vA | neti pakShe.anubhavavirodhastadabhidhAnavaiyarthyaM cha | Adye brahmalakShaNamapi kathaM na jIvavyAvR^ittiM karoti | kathaM cha tatsambandhena saguNaM na bhavatIti | maivam.h | yo hi kAryakAraNasaN^ghAtAdavivikttaM kartR^itvabhokttR^itvadoShasaMsargiNamAtmAnaM matvA klishyati sa jIvo vyAvartyata eva te(ane)na lakShaNena | tatra yashchaitanyadhAtuH sa brahmaNo na bhidyata ityabhyupagame virodhAbhAvAt.h | nacha satyasya prapaJNchasya kAraNabhUtAyAH satyAyA mAyAyA Ashrayo brahmeti sUtrArtho yena brahmaNaH savisheShatvaM syAt.h | kintu yadavaShyambho vishvo vivartaH prapaJNchastad.h brahmeti sUtrArthaH | sati chaivaM sUtrArthe kathaM jIvabrahmaNorekatvaM brahmaNo nirguNatvaM cha viruddhayata iti | 
atrochyate | AstAM tAvat.h(eShA) prapaJNchasya vivartatA.a.adivArtA pramANAbhAvAt.h prakR^ityadhikaraNe nirAkariShyamANatvAchcha | taTasthena jagajjanmAdikAraNatvenAtra sUtre lakShaNayA brahma pratipAdyata iti kuto.aN^gIkaraNIyam.h | mukhyArthAsambhave hi lakShaNAshrayaNaM dR^iShyam.h | na tAvad.h brahmaNo jagajjanmAdikAraNatvasya bAdhakaM pratyakShaM tadagocharatvAt.h | nApyanumAnam.h shrutibAdhitatvAt.h | nApyAgamaH tasyAkliShyakAritvAdyarthatayA sAvakAshatvAt.h | 
nanvarthApattyedamavasIyate | jIvabrahmaNorekatvaM tAvadAvashyakam.h | nacha jagajjanmAdikAraNatvasya svalakShaNatve tatsambhavati | ato.anyathA.anupapattyA mAyAgatamevedaM lakShaNam.h | janmAdyasya yatastad.h brahmeti lakShaNayochyata iti kalpyata iti | tatrAha- bhedenaiveti || 
yadi jIvabrahmaNorekatvaparirakShaNAya yathAshrutaM sUtrArthaM parityajya lakShaNA.ashrIyate tarhi jIvabrahmaNorbhedenaivAN^gIkR^itena sUtrasya mukhyArthasambhave lakShaNA kasmAdAshrayaNIyA | 
nanvabhedamupAdAya sUtre lakShaNA vA.a.ashrayaNIyA bhedamupAdAya makhyavR^ittirveti sandihyate | vayaM tu brUmaH dvitIyaH pakSha eva shreyAniti, aprAmANikaparirakShaNAya vAkyAnAM jaghanyavR^ittirAshrIyamANA kvachi(dupalabdheti)dapi dR^iShyeti | tadidamukttaM- bhedenaiveti ||
nanu kathaM jIvabrahmaikyamaprAmANikam.h | tattvamasItyAdishrutisiddhami(tvAdi)ti chenna | upapattiparAhatatvAt.h | tathAhi | tachChabdenA(bdasya) mukhyArtho yaH, "sadeva somya' ityAdinA prakR^itaH prekShApUrvaM tejo.abannAdInAM sraShyA sarvAsAM prajAnAM mUlamAyatanaM pratiShThA cha sakalAvadyagandhavidhuro.aparichChinnaguNAkaraH paramAtmA, yashcha tvaMpadamukhyArthaH pratyakSha(Adi)siddho.alpashakttiH parAdhIno doShakaluShito.avachChinnaj~nAnAdiguNaH, tAvupAdAyAnena vAkyenaikyamuchyate, uta viruddhabhAgatyAgena lakShaNayA vA | nAdyaH | parasparavirodhena yogyatAvirahe jaradgavAdivAkyavadAbhAsatvaprasaN^gAt.h | dvitIye doShamAha- bhedanaiveti || 
siMho devadatta ityAdivatsAmAnAdhikaraNyamAtraM gauNamupAdAya jIvabrahmaNorbhede(nA)naivAN^gIkR^itena padadvayasya mukhyArtha(tva)sambhave(na) jahadajahallakShaNA kuta AshrayaNIyeti | 
nanu kiM sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM mukhyamupAdAya tattvaMpadayorlAkShaNikatvaM vyAkhyeyam.h | kiMvA sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM gauNaM gR^ihItvA tattvaMpadayormukhyArthatA vyAkhyAtavyeti sandehe na vinigamanAyAM heturasti | na nAsti | tyajedekaM kulasyArtha iti nyAyasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | tAtparyaliN^gAnAM tatratatra bheda evAnuguNyasya vyutpAditatvAt.h | tadidamukttaM - bhedenaiveti ||
kiJNcha virodhyAkAraparityAgena svarUpamAtralakShaNayA "tattvamasi' iti vAkyaM jIvabrahmaNorekatvaM pratipAdayatItyatra virodhyAkAraparityAgo nAma na tAvadavivakShAmAtramityukttaM prAk.h | atha so.ayaM devadatta ityAdivadvirodhyAkArasyAnityatvam.h | tatrAha- kathamiti || 
nityaguNatvaM cheshvarasya liN^gapAde sAdhayiShyate | asyeshvarasyetyupalakShaNam.h | jIve.api pAratantAdidoShANAM nityatvAt.h | yathokttaM purANe "alpashakttirasArvaj~nam.h' iti | 
nanu cha virodhyAkAraparityAgena jIvasya brahmaikyamityasyArtho na virodhyAkArAvivakShAmAtreNeti nApyanityatveneti | kintu nigaruNena brahmaNA jIvasyaikyamityeveti chenna | nirguNa(tva)syaiva nirUpayitumashakyatvAt.h | tathAhi | tannirguNaM kiM saguNAdIshvarAdbhinnamutAbhinnam.h(vA) | dvitIye tasyApi saguNatvaprasaN^gena nirguNatvavyAghAtaH | Adye doShamAha- sadaiveti || 
yadi nirguNaM saguNAdatyantabhinnaM tarhyasya saguNasya nityaM saguNatvAttasmAnnityameva nirguNaM bhinnaM prasajyeta | tathAcha na kadAchidapi kaivalyaM syAditi |

nanu guNAdipaJNchakasya nirguNatvaM padArthavido manyante | manyantAm.h | na hIdAnIM nirguNavastunirAkaraNaM prastutam.h | kiM nAmAdvaidinA nirguNaM brahma nirUpayitumashakyamiti | guNashabdenA(chA)tra dharmamAtraM prakR^itam.h | tadguNAdiShvapi sarvasammatam.h | guNAdInAM cha saguNatvaM paramANvArambhanirAse vakShyate |

tadA cha yuktayA nirgu(Ne)Natve nirAkR^ite.api yadi nirguNatvaM parasmai ruchiM syAt.h tarhi guNashabdoditasakalashubharAhityalakShaNamAsuratvameva syAt.h | anyathAnirUpayitumashakyatvasyokttatvAt.h | tenaikyaM cha mAyAvAdinAmanumanyAmaha iti | etena brahmaNo nirguNatvAdasya lakShaNasya yattaTasthatvamukttam.h | nahi nAnAvidhakAryakriyAveshAtmatvaM tatprasavashaktayatmakaM vA jij~nAsyavishuddhabrahmAntargataM bhavitumarhati | tadapi nirastaM veditavyam.h | nirguNa(tva)syaiva nirAkR^itatvAt.h | yachchokttam.h "nedaM brahmaNo visheShaNam.h prapaJNchopAdhitvena nirupAdhikabrahmasvarUpAntargatatvAyogAt.h' iti, taduttaratra nirAkariShyata iti |

yadatra jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM mu(khya)khato lakShaNamabhihitaM savarj~natvAdisamastaguNavattvaM chAbhiprAyavyA(prA)ptamityukttam.h | tadubhayamapi lakShaNaM lakShyAdbrahmaNo bhinnamabhinnaM bhinnAbhinnaM vA | nAdyaH | merumandaravallakShyalakShaNabhAvasya guNaguNibhAvasya chAnupapatteH | sambandhasadbhAvAnneti chet.h (na) tasyApi sambandhibhyAmanyatvAnanyatvAbhyAmanirUpaNAt.h | na dvitIyaH | anekairabhinnasya brahmaNo.apyanekatvApatteH | tathA chaikameveti shrutivirodhAt.h | lakShaNAnAM vaikatvamApadyeta | tathAcha "yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante' ityAdishruteH punarukttidoShaprasaN^gaH | lakShyalakShaNabhAvo guNaguNibhAvashchAbhede nopapadyate | prasiddhena hyaprasiddhaM lakShaNIyam.h | nacha tadeva tadaiva prasiddhamaprasiddhaM cheti yukttam.h | guNI cha guNavAnbhavati | nacha svenaiva tadvAnbhavati | na tR^itIyaH | parasparavirodhAt.h | ato.ashakyanirUpaNatvAnnedaM brahmasvarUpAntargataM lakShaNam.h | kintu taTasthameva | nacha taTasthena tena brahmaNo.advitIyatvabhaN^gaH | yadrajatamityabhAtsA shukttiritivanmithyAbhUtenApi prapaJNchakAraNatvenopalakShaNayogAditi | 
evamanUdya nirAkartumArabhate- iti pR^iShya iti || 
vakttavyamiti sheShaH | pR^iShya itayupalakShaNam.h | dUShite chetyapi grAhyam.h | dUShaNAnAmatyantAsambaddhatvAtpR^iShya ityevokttam.h | kiM vakttavyamiti | 
tatra jagajjanmAdikAraNatvAdInAM dharmANAM bhedAbhAve.api visheShasya sadbhAvAttadbalena sarvamutpadyata iti vakttuM nirbhedavastuni pareNa visheShasyAnaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h ghaTAdInAM cha mithyAtvenAN^gIkR^itAnAmanudAharaNatvAtsatya eva vastunyasAvudapapAdanIya iti manvAna Aha- tadeti || 
yadyevaM pR^iShTvA lakShaNaM dUShayasi tadaikyasya gatirnirUpaNaprakAro na vidyate | 
ayamabhiprAyaH | dvividhaM hi vAkyaM mAyAvAdinA tattvAvedakamaN^gIkR^itam.h | ekaM jIvabrahmaNoraikyaparaM mahAvAkyam.h | yathA tattvamasItyAdi | aparaM tatsvarUpaparamavAntaravAkyam.h | yathA satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahmetyAdi | tadubhayamapi savisheShAbhinnavastuniShThaM pareNAN^gIkaraNIyam.h | gatyantarAbhAvAt.h | 
tatra tAvadAdyasya gatyantaraM nAsti | kathamiti chet.h uchyate | tattvamasItyAdivAkyapratipAdyamaikyaM kiM tatpadalakShitAchchaitanyAdabhinnamuta bhinnamatha bhinnAbhinnamiti vAchyam.h | 
pareNAN^gIkR^itatvena prAdhAnyAdabhedapakShaM tAvadAdau nirAkaroti- aikyAbheda iti || 
aikyasya chaitanyasvarUpAbhede.aN^gIkriyamANe tadaikyaM tattvamasItyAdinA shAstreNa pratipAdyaM na syAt.h | kutaH svarUpasya svaprakAshatvena nityasiddhatvAt.h | tanmAtrasvarUpatvAchchaikyasya | nahi prakAshamAnameva shAstrapratipAdyam.h | vaiyarthyaprasaN^gAt.h | kiJNchAvedyatve satyaparokShavyavahArayogyatvaM svaprakAshatvaM paroNAN^gIkR^itam.h | tathAcha svaprakAshachaitanyAtmakaM (cha) shAstrapratipAdyaM cheti vyAhatam.h | atha shAstraM naikyaM pratipAdayati kintu bhedabhramaM nirAkaroti, yathokttam.h siddhaM tu nivartakatvAditi | na | aikye prakAshamAne bhedabhramasyaivAnavakAshAt.h | tattvApratipatterbhrAntihetutvAt.h | aikyaM na prakAshata iti chenna | svaprakAshachaitanyamAtratvavirodhAt.h | avidyAvashAtsvaprakAshasyApyanavabhAsa iti chenna sarvathA.apyanavabhAsaprasaN^gAt.h | tathAchAdhiShThAnAnavabhAse.avidyAropasyApyanupapatteH | na hyakhaNDe vastunyaMshato.avidyAvaraNaM sambhavati | asambhavanIyAvabhAsachaturA.avidyeti chet.h | tarhi sA jaDeShveva kuto nAN^gIkAryA | anupapattestulyatvAt.h | tathAcha "sA na jaDeShu vastuShu' ityayukttam.h | na shAstreNa j~neyaM tadityupalakShaNam.h | shAstrapratipAdyatve.api tatpadenaiva siddhatvAt.h | tvamasIti vyarthamityapi draShyavyam.h | tadityetAvatA na bhedabhramanivR^ittiH | atastvamasIti sArthakamiti chenna | tatpadenai(vai)kyasya pratipAditatvAdaikyapratItau cha bhedabhramasya nirastatvAt.h | anyathA kadA.apyanivR^ittiprasaN^gAt.h | tatpadenaikyasyApratipAditatve tadupalakShitachaitanyamAtratvAnupapattiH | nanu kathaM tarhi so.ayaM devadatta iti vAkyam.h | atrApi visheShAnaN^gIkAre.anupapattireveti | 
dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- bheda iti || aikyasya svarUpAdbhede.aN^gIkriyamANe.apasiddhAntastAvat.h | tattvamasyAdivAkyasyAkhaNDArthaniShThatAyA mAyAvAdinAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | mithyAtvaprasaN^go.aparo doShaH, chaitanyAtirikttasya sarvasya mithyAtvAN^gIkArAt.h | anyathA.advaitenaiva satyenAdvaitavyAghAtAt.h | aikyamithyAtve kinnashChinnamiti chenna | mithyAtvato na shAstreNa j~neyaM tadityanuvartanAt.h | anyathA tattvamasyAdishAstrasyAtattvAvedakatvaM syAt.h | kiJNcha jIvabrahmaNoraikyasya mithyAtvatastadbhedasatyatvamapi syAt.h | kutaH balAdvayAptibalAdityarthaH | nanu na kutrApi satayo bhedo.asmAbhirabhyupeyate tatkathaM vyAptiH | maivam.h | AstAM tAvatparamArthachintA | yayordUrasthayorvanaspatyoraikyaM mithyA tayorbhedaH satya iti dR^iShyam.h | athavA yasya svarUpeNa sato yo.abhAvo mithyA tasya tadviparItaH satyo yathA brahmaNo.anR^itatvAdermithyAtve satyatvAdikaM satyamiti sAmAnyavyAptyAshrayaNena prasaN^gopapattiH yathAhuH "parasparavirodhe tu na prakArAntarasthitiH' iti | 
tR^itIyaM nirAchaShye- bhedAbhedAviti ||
jIvabrahmaNoraikyasya svarUpAdbhedAbhedau yadyaN^gIkriyete | tadA vakttavyaM tau kiM chaitanyAdabhinnAvuta bhinnau atha bhinnAbhinnAviti | Adye chaitanyasyApi dvitvaM tayorvaikatvamityAdyApadyeta | dvitIyayordoShamAha- tadeti || 
hishabdenAnavasthAvyutpAdanAya spaShyatAmAchaShye | tathA hi | sa bhedaH kiM bhedibhyAM bhinno.abhinno bhinnAbhinno vA | prathame so.api bhedastathetyanavasthA | dvitIye shabdaparyAyatvAdayo doShAH | tR^itIyastu tR^itIye.antarbhavati | tatrApyukttavidhayA.anavasthaiveti | 
nanu bhedasya bhedAntaraM bhedAbhedayoshcha bhedAbhedAntaramityetAvatA nAnavasthA | utpattij~naptipratibandhakatvAbhAvAditi chenna | visheSheNapratItimantareNa vishiShyapratyayAnupapattyA j~naptipratibandhakatvAt.h | tadidamukttaM-syAdeveti || yadyapi bhedAbhedAN^gIkAre virodho vakttuM shakyate tathA.api sphuTatvAnnokttaH | evamaikyasya svarUpAdbhedapakShe.anavasthA.apIti |
nanvaikyaM chaitanyAbhinnamapi svanirvAhakatvAtsvAbhAvikaprakAshenAprakAshitatvamAtmano nirvakShyati(hiShyati) | yadvA svarUpeNaikyasya bhedAbhedau stAm.h | 
tayoshcha bhedAbhedAntarAbhAve.api svanirvAhakatvAdvayavahAropapattiriti chenna | visheShAnabhyupagame svanirvAhakatvasyApi vakttumashakyatvAdityabhiprAyeNAha- svanirvAhakateti || 
aikyasya bhedAbhedayorvA svanirvAhakatA yadyaN^gIkR^itA syAt.h | tadA pR^ichChAmaH svasya nirvAhakaM hi svanirvAhakaM tasya bhAvaH svanirvAhakatA | svasyeti cha karmaNi ShaShThI | kartR^ikarmaNoH kR^itIti vachanAt.h | tathA chaikasyaivaikasyAmeva nirvAhakriyAyAM karmakartR^itvalakShaNaM nirvAhyatvaM nirvAhakatvamityukttaM bhavati | tannirvAhyatvaM nirvAhakatvaM cha parasparaM dharmiNA kriyayA chAtyantAbhinnamu(tAtyaM)tabhi(nnAbhi)nnamiti | 
nirvAhyamiti nirvAhakamiti apishabdAnnirvAhakamityapi shabdasamUhaH payarAyaH prasajyeta ekArthatvAt.h | nacha teShAM shabdAnAM kashchitparyAyatvaM manyate | 
dvitIyamanUdya dUShayati- bhedavAniti || 
vAshabdo yadyarthe | yadi nirvAhyatvAdirarthaH parasparaM dharmiNA na bhedavAn.h syAttadA tadbhedadvayasya bhedisvarUpamAtratve paryAyatvAdidoShaprasaN^gAdbhedAntaravadityaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | tathAcha parasparaM bhedaM dharmibhedaM vA.a.ashrityobhayatrAnavasthA syAditi | 
evaM visheShAnabhyupagame mahAvAkyArthAnupapattimabhidhAyAvAntaravAkye.api tAmatidishati- satyeti ||
satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahmetyAdike.avAntaravAkye.apyevaM vikalpya dUShaNamabhidhAnIyamityarthaH | tathAhi | satyaj~nAnAdikaM parasparaM brahmaNA chAtyantAbhinnaM vA bhinnaM vA bhinnAbhinnaM vA | nAdyaH | tathA sati svaprakAshabrahmAtmakasya tasya satyaj~nAnAdishAstrapratipAdyatvaprasaN^gAt.h | satyaj~nAnAdipadAnAM paryAyatvApattyA sahaprayogAnupapattiprasaN^gAchcha | na dvitIyaH | apasiddhAntAt.h | mithyAtvApattyA shAstrasyAtattvAvedakatvaprasaN^gAchcha | aj~nAnatvAdeH satyatvApatteshcha | na tR^itIyaH | anavasthAprasaN^gAt.h | svanirvAhakatvasya chokttavidhayA nirvakttumashakyatvAditi | 
nanu satyaj~nAnAdInAM parasparaM brahmaNA chAtyantamabheda eva | nacha tAvatA satyaj~nAnAdipadAnAM paryAyatvam.h | vAchyArthabhedasadbhAvAt.h | parAparasAmAnyavAchinAM saguNabrahmavAchinAM vA teShAM parabrahmaNi lakShaNayA pravR^ittyaN^gIkArAt.h | nacha vAchyaM satyapadena lakShitasyaiva j~nAnapadena lakShaNAyAM vaiyarthyAt.h, adhikalakShaNAyAM cha nAkhaNDArthatAsiddhiriti | lakShyArthabhedAbhAve.apyAropitAsatyatvAdivyavR^ittyarthatvenapadAntarANAM saprayojanatvAt.h | ata eva na shAstravaiyarthyam.h | svaprakAshe.apyAropitAkAravyAvR^ittyarthatvena shAstrasya saprayojanattvAditi chenna | kiM brahmavisheShaNatvenAsatyatvAdivyAvR^ittibodhaH prayojanamuchyate | kiMvA svatantra eva vyAvR^ittibodhaH | 
Adye doShamAha- na vyAvR^ittyeti || 
itthambhUtalakShaNe tR^itIyA | brahmavisheShaNatvenAsatyatvAdivyAvR^ittilakShaNaM prayojanaM satyAdipadAnAM tvayA vakttuM na shakyate | kuta ityata Aha- vyAvR^ittasyeti || vyAvR^ittatayA pratItasya brahmaNo.avisheShatve satItyarthaH | abhAvavisheShAN^gIkAre cha bhAvavisheShaiH kimaparAddham.h | 
dvitIyaM dUShayati- na vyAvR^ittasyeti || vyAvR^ittervyAvR^ittasya brahmaNo.avisheShatve sA svatantrA vyAvR^ittirna prayojanam.h | ajij~nAsitatvAt.h | mumukShuNA brahma vA taddharmo vA jij~nAsitavyaH | tatra vyAvR^ittirna brahma | tasya bhAvarUpatvAdekatvAnnirupAdhikatvAchcha | brahmadharmo.api na chetkathaM mumukShuNA jij~nAsyeta | ajij~nAsitabodhanaM cha kathaM prayojanaM syAditi | 
kiJNcha satyAdipadAni brahmaNi kiM satyatvAdidharmAnAbhidadhatyasattvAdivyAvR^ittiprayojanAni | utAnyathA vA | 
nAdyaH | anaN^gIkArAdityAha- na vyAvR^ittyeti || vyAvR^ittasya brahmaNo.avisheShatve.aN^gIkR^ite sati, visheShaNAbhidhAnamukhena vyAvR^ittiH padAnAM prayojanamiti vakttuM na shakyata ityarthaH | 
dvitIyaM dUShayati- na vyAvR^ittasyeti || vyAvR^ittasya brahmaNo.avisheShatve satyatvAdidharmApratipAdana iti yAvat.h | asatyatvAdivyAvR^ittiH padAnAM prayojanamiti vakttuM na shakyate | nahi tIre nadItvamanabhidadhato nadIpadasyAnadItvavyAvR^ittiH prayojanaM sambhavati | virodhyAkArasamarpaNena hi virodhyAkArAntaraM vyAvartanIyam.h | 
yadukttaM shAstraM chAropitAkAravyAvR^ittyA svaprakAshe.api prayojanavaditi | tadapyanenaiva nirastam.h | nirvisheShe svayaMprakAshamAne virodhyAkArAropa evAnupapanna iti chokttam.h | 
evaM visheShAnaN^gIkAre vAkyadvayasyAnupapattimabhidhAyopasaMharati- taditi || 
tattasmAdakhaNDaM nirvisheShaM vAkyadvayapratipAdyamityetanmataM khaNDitaM dUShitaM veditavyamityarthaH | 
svakriyAviruddhaM cha nirvisheShatvavachanamityAha- nirvisheShatvamiti || yathA mUko.ahamityetatsvakriyAviruddham.h | vakttR^itvAbhAvo hyanenochyate vachanakriyayA cha vakttR^itvamiti | tathA nirvisheShaM brahmeti svakriyAviruddhaM bhavet.h | katham.h | etena nirvisheShatvena visheSheNApatitena hetunA | visheShAbhAvo hi nirvisheShaM brahmeti vAkyena pratipAdayitumiShyaH | pratipAdanakriyayA cha visheShAbhAvalakShaNo visheShaH prApnotIti | ayamapi visheSho nirvisheShamityanena nirAkriyata iti kutastatrApi svakriyAvirodhaH | pratItivirodha iti chet.h | tarhyetadvachanakartR^itvamapi mUko.ahamityanena nirAkriyata iti kutastatrApi svakriyAvirodhaH | pratItivirodha iti chet.h | samassamAdhiH | parabodhanopAyAbhAvAdvisheShAbhAva upAdIyate | natu brahmavisheShatayeti chet.h | atrApi parabodhanopAyAbhAvAdevedaM vachanam.h | vastutastvasau mUka evetyastu | nirvisheSham.h ityasya visheShanirAsa eva tAtparyam.h | na nirvisheShatvavisheShavidhau |ataH kathaM virodha iti chet.h | tarhi mUko.ahamityasyApi vakttR^itvanirAse tAtparyam.h | naitadvachanavakttR^itva iti kutastatrApi virodhaH | na tatra svavachanavirodhaH | kintu svakriyAvirodha iti chet.h | prakR^ite.api kimanyo.abhihita ityAstAM prapaJNchaH | tadidamukttaM- mUko.ahamitivaditi || 
yadarthamayaM prayatnastadAha- abhinne.apIti || ata ukttaprakAreNa mahAvAkyAvAntaravAkyayoranyathA.anupapattibalAdbhedarahite.api brahmaNyayamanupapattishAntiheturvisheSho nAma shakttivisheSho.aN^gIkaraNIyaH prApnoti | idamukttaM bhavati | mahAvAkyapratipAdyamaikyamavAntaravAkyapratipAdyaM cha satyatvAdikaM brahmaNA parasparaM chAbhinnameva | ekadhaivAnudraShyavyamityAdyekarasa(tva)pratipAdakashruteH | na chokttadoShaH | yato bhedahIne.api vastunyasti kashchichChakttivisheSho yena prakAshamAnamapi na prakAshata ityAdi yujyate | sa cha visheSho.anayaivArthApattyA.avagamyata ityeva tvayA vakttavyamiti | 
nanvaN^gIkR^ite.api visheShe nAnupapattishAntiH | so.api hi visheSho yadi vastuno bhinnastarhi bhedAnavasthAdi doShaH syAdabhinnatve cha visheShatadvadbhAvAnupapattestAdavasthyAdityata Aha- visheSheti || visheShavisheShiNoshchAbheda evAN^gIkaraNIyaH | visheShabalAchcha visheShatadvadbhAvo.apyupapAdanIya iti sheShaH | tathA.api visheShaparasparayA.anavasthA syAdityata Aha- svanirvAhakateti || sa eva visheSho visheShAntaramantareNa visheShatadvadbhAvaM cha ghaTayati | ekasyaiva nirvAhyatvaM nirvAhakatvaM cha tadbalAdeva siddhayatItyaN^gIkaraNIyamiti | 
nanvabhinne vastuni bhedakAryanirvAhakatvaM visheShasya kutaH pramANAt.h(taH) siddhamityata Aha- bhedahIne tviti || tushabdo.avadhAraNe | aparyAyashabdAntaraniyAmaka ityasheShabhedakAyarnirvAhakatvopalakShaNam.h | etadukttaM bhavati | jIvabrahmaikyAdInAmekadhaivetyAdishrutyA chaitanyasvarUpamAtratvaM pratIyate | chaitanye svaprakAshatayA siddhe.apyasiddhiraparyAyashabdavedyatvam.h, chaitanyaprakAshasya nAvidyAnivartakatvamadvaitaj~nAnasya tannivartakatvamityarthakriyavisheShaH | chaitanyamekaM satyatvAdInyanekAnIti saN^khayAvailakShaNyamityAdibhedakAryANi chAvagamyate | etadubhayAnyathA.anupapattyA bhedarahite.api chaitanye bhedrapratinidhistatkAyarkArI kashchidatishayo.astIti kalpyate | gatyantarAbhAvAt.h | tathAchArthApattyA svarUpagrAhiNyA bhedakAryanirvAhaka eva(cha)Asau siddha iti kiM tatra pramANAntarAnveShaNeneti | anenaiva visheShasya lakShaNaM chokttaM bhavati | bhedahAne.apyanupacharitabhedavyavahAranimittaM visheSha iti | 
evamadvaitavAdinA visheShamaN^gIkArayitvA.anyAnapyaN^gIkArayati- so.astIti || na kevalaM brahmaNi mAyAvAdinA visheSho.aN^gIkaraNIyaH | kiM nAma prapaJNchasatyatAvAdibhirapyasheShadravyeShu sa visheSho.aN^gIka(rtavyaH)AryaH | tathA hi paTastachChauklayaM cha tAvanna bhidyete | aN^gulIdvayavadbhedenAnupalambhAt.h | ayutasiddhatvAditi chet.h | kimayutasiddhatvaM nAma | avashyamAshrayAshrayibhAvenAvasthAnamiti chet.h | kimetAvatA bhedena na pratyetavyam.h | nApi kuNDamiva paTo.adhikaraNatvena badarANIva shauklayamAdheyatvena parisphurati | kiM nAma tadeva taditi | na chaiShA pratItirbhrAntiH | bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | shauklayapaTayorbhedAvagAhinI pratyakShapratItirhi bAdhikA bhavet.h | anumAnAdInAmabhedapratyaya(kSha)rodhenotthAnasyaivAsambhavAt.h | nacha bhedAvagAhinI pratyakShapratItirastItyukttam.h | tena pratyakShata eva siddhaH paTashauklayayorabhedaH | dR^ishyante cha bhedakAryANi, paTashauklayabuddhayoranyUnAnatirikttaviShayatvAbhAvaH, tachChabdayoraparyAyatvaM aparyAyashabdasmArakatvaM, jalAharaNAdyarthakriyAbhedaH, paTamAnayetyuktte yatkiJNchichChuklayAnAnayanaM, shuklamAnayetyuktte niyamena paTasyAnayanam.h, apaTaH paTa itivadashuklaH paTa ityanayorvirodhAbhAvaH, andhasyApi paTo.ayamitivachChuklo.ayamiti cha pratItyanutpattiH, shuklApratipattivatpaTApratipattyabhAvaH, mahArajanasamparkeNa shuklatvavatpaTasyA(pyA)vR^ittatvAbhAvaH, paTavadvA shauklayasyApyanAvR^ittatvAbhAvaH, ityevamAdIni | nachaiShA pratItirbhAntiH | bAdhitatvAbhimAnasyApyabhAvAt.h | vyavahArAdyavisaMvAdAchcha tadetayorabhedabhedakAryapratItyoranyathA.anupapattyA nirbhede.api paTe.asti kashchidatishayo bhedapratinidhiryadvashAdidaM sarvaM samaJNjasaM syAdityeva kalpanIyam.h | na chAtishayo.abhinne.api visheShakatvAdvisheSha iti gIyate | evamanyatrApi dravye visheShaH pratipattavyaH | 
nanu bhedAbhedAN^gIkAreNAnupapatteH shamanAt.h kiM visheSheNeti chenna | parasparaviruddhayorbhedAbhedayorekatrAvasthAnaghaTanAyA(ma)pi visheShasyApyaN^gIkaraNIyatvAt.h | pratItatvAtko virodha iti chet.h | satyam.h | pratItirapi kathamupapanneti chintAyAM vastusvabhAvAtishayasyAnusaraNIyatvAt.h | bhedAbhedAnavasthAparihArArthamapi visheShAN^gIkArasyAvashyakatvasyokttatvAditi | 
nanu sarvavastuShu yadyasti visheShaH, sa cha vastuno na bhidyate, prAptaM tarhi sakalavastUnAmaikyamityata Aha- visheShA iti ||
te prakR^itasvarUpA visheShA asheShato vastuShvananteShu dravyeShvanantA eva santi | na punareka eva sarvatrAto nokttadoShaH | so.astItyekavachanaM tu samudAyApekShayA prayukttamiti bhAvaH | nanvekaikasmiMshcha dravye visheSho.apyekaiko.asti tadA paTo mahAMshChuklashchalatIti vichitrAnekavyavahArAnupapattiH | na hyekasmAdavichitrasvabhAvAdvichitrAnekakAryotpattirdR^iShyA | tathA satyAkasmikatvaprasaN^gAt.h | tatashcha visheShAN^gIkAro vyarthaH syAdityata Aha- visheShA iti || 
te.apyukttalakShaNA visheShA asheShato.api vastuShu pratyekamanantAH santyato nokttadoShAvakAshaH anantA ityupalakShaNam.h | yatra yAvanto vyavahArAstatra tAvanto visheShA iti j~nAtavyam.h | 
pratidravyamanekatve visheShANAM parasparaM bhedena bhAvyam.h | bhedAvinAbhUtatvAdanekatvasya | tathAcha bhinnanAM dravyAbhede dravyasyApi bhedaprasaN^ga ityata Aha- parampareti || parasparavisheShavattvenaivAnekatvaM sambhavati | visheShasya bhedakAryakAritAyA ukttatvAditi bhAvaH | 
visheShANAmapi visheShAntarAN^gIkAre.anavasthetyata Aha- svanirvAhakateti || pUrvaM dravyeNa visheShasyAbhedachintA | idAnIM tu parasparamiti sphuTo.arthabhedaH | sarvaM chaitadvisheShasvarUpasAdhakArthApattyaiva siddhamiti na pR^ithak.h pramANamukttam.h | nahi svayamanupapannamanupapattyantarashAntyai prabhavati | kintu yathAyathopapadyate tathAtathaiva svarUpagrAhiNyA.arthApatyaiva kalpyate | yadyapi visheShaH pratyakSho.api bhavati | "yena pratyakShasiddhena' iti vakShyamANatvAt.h | tathA.api vipratipanno na tanmAtreNa bodhayituM shakyata ityarthApattirupanyasteti | 
yadarthaM tadaikyasyetyAdinA sarvavAdibhirvisheSho.aN^gIkAritastadidAnImAha- ata iti ||

nanvatraivaM prayokttavyam.h, IshvaraH kiJNchijj~naH paMratvAddevadattavaditi | tatreshvaraH pramito vA na vA | Adye yena pra(yatpra)mANena siddhastenaiva tasya sArvaj~nasiddherdharmigrAhaka(pramANa)virodhaH | dvitIye tvAshrayAsiddhiH | tatkathamuchyate IshituH kiJNchijj~natvaM cha puMstvena sAdhayituM shakyaM hIti tatrAha- sukhamiti || tatkathamityata ukttaM- vanakR^ittvAdirUpeNa pakShabhUtasyeti || prasiddhakartR^irahitaM vanaM sakartR^ikaM kAryatvAdityAdinA yo vanAdikartA siddhaH tenaivAkAreNa taM pakShIkR^itya prayoge na ko.api doSha ityAshayaH | vanakR^ittvaM parvatAdhArakatvamityAdirUpo dharmastenopetasya | nahi vanakartetyetAvatA sarvaj~na iti labhyate | prasiddhavanakarturasarvaj~natvAt.h | sa evakShityAdikarteti kathaM na sArvaj~nyamiti chenna | tadbhAve pramANAbhAvAt.h | nahi kAryatvAdihetuH kartAramiva tasya sarvatraikatvaM gamayituM shaknoti | lAghavAdekatvamAshrIyata iti chet.h(na) | lokadarshanAnusAreNa kartAraM kalpayato gauravAshrayaNasyaivo(syo)chitatvAt.h | loke hi gajagavayagardabhAdInAM ghaTAdInAM cha nirmAtAro vijAtIyA evopalabhyante | nacha vanakartA kiJNchijj~na iti sAdhane kimIshvarasyeti vAchyam.h | tasya cheshvaratAyAH pareNa | anyathA vanakartari siddhe kimIshvarasiddhAvAyAtamityapi syAt.h |

chitriNI vandhyA | ShaShTho raso rasAntaravAnityuktte prathamAdirasena siddhasAdhanaM syAt.h | saptamarasavAnityuktte aprasiddhavisheShaNatA syAt.h | ataH sottara ityukttam.h | IshvarAnumAnasya pramANatAyAmeteShAmapi prAmANyaM syAditi sheShaH | nanu vastutvaM ghaTAdAvanaikAntikamiti chenna | tasyApi pakShatvAt.h | turagR^iN^gAdInAmanupalambhabAdha iti chet.h | kShityAdisakarturapyevameva | ayogyatvAnnopalabhyata iti chet.h | turagaviShANamapi evama(mevA)stu | na cha(nu) viShANaM nAma mahattve satyudbhUtarUpa(H) sharIrAvayavavisheShaH | sa kathamupalabdhyayogyaH syAditi chet.h | kartA.api tarhi kulAlAdiriva mahattve satyadbhutarUpasharIravAnkathamupalabdhyayogyo bhaviShyati | asharIratvAnnopalabhyata iti chet.h | rUpAbhAvAtturagaviShANamapi tathA.astu | viShANaM rUpavadeveti chet.h | kartA.api sharIravAneva | sharIraM kartR^itve.anupayukttamiti chet.h na | kimupayogena | na hi tadutpattyA vyAptirbauddhAnAmiva bhavatAm.h | dharmAdimattvaM sharIritve prayojakamiti chenna | tasyApi kartR^itvena sAdhanAditi | nanu kathamatra prayokttavyam.h | anumAnatvaM yadi kAryatvAdau varteta tadA tadavishiShye vastutvAdau(api) vartetetyevamiti | 
nanu vichArashAstramArabhya jagatkAraNe.anumAnAnavakAshavyutpAdanaM vyAhatamityAshaN^kAM pariharannupasaMharati- upakramAdIti ||
AgamAnugR^ihItAnumAnopalakShaNametat.h | AgamAnugrahe hi sarvANyetAnyanumAnAnyeva | pakShadharmatAdInAmaN^gAnAmapauruSheyatayA svataH pramANena shAstreNa siddheH | pratipakShAdInAM cha tadvirodhena bAdhAditi saN^kShepaH | tadevaM jagatkAraNatvasya (Nasya) shAstraikasamadhigamyatvAnnAnumAnAdinA 
lakShaNasyAtivyAptikathanaM yukttamiti siddham.h | 
atra kechit.h shAstrasya yoniriti vyAchakSha(kR^irva)te | tadanupapannam.h prakR^itAnupayogAt.h | nahi shAstrakAraNatvaM jagatkAraNatve hetuH | vyAptyadarshanAt.h | pUvarsUtre jagatkAraNatvena pratItaM sArvaj~naM brahmaNo vedakAraNatvena sphuTIkriyata iti chenna | vedasyApi sakalajagadantarbhAvAt.h | kathaM chAnantapadArthAtmakasya prapaJNchasya kartR^itvena na sphuTaM tadekadeshavedakAraNatvena sphuTIbhaviShyati sArvaj~nam.h | atha jagatkAraNatvaM pradhAnAdivyudAsena brahmaNyeva sAdhayituM hetutvenokttaM sArvaj~naM shAstrayonitvena sAdhyata iti chenna | asiddhiprasaN^gAt.h | nahi brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvamanaN^gIkuvarANo vedakAraNatvamaN^gIkaroti | Agamena sAdhyata iti chet.h | tarhi jagatkAraNatvameva tena kiM na sAdhyate | IkShatyadhikaraNAdinA janmAdisUtrasya punarukttaprasaN^gAchcha | jagatkAraNatvena savarj~natvaM na siddhayati vedAkartR^itvAdityAshaN^kayedamukttamiti chenna | tathA sati pratij~nAmAtratvaprasaN^gAt.h | viyadAdiviShayepyevamAshaN^kAprasaN^gAt.h | viyadadhikaraNAdau sA.api nirAkariShyata iti chet.h na | tarhi tenaivedaM gatArthaM syAt.h |
kiJNcha vedakartR^itvAbhAve(na) sArvaj~nyaM na sambhavatIti shaN^kaiva nirdalA | nahi tatkatraraiva tajj~nAtavyamiti niyamo.asti | kiJNcha vedakartR^itvaM kathaM sArvaj~nyasAdhakam.h | yo yAvadarthapratipAdakasya vAkyasya praNetA sa tato.apyadhikamarthaM jAnAtyeva | yathA pANinyAdiH | ayaM chAsheShArthapratipAdakasya shAstrasya praNetA.ataH kathaM na sarvatra iti chet.h na | kimidaM vedapraNetR^itvaM nAma | kiM pramANAntareNArthamupalabhya svechChayA (padAdini)prabandha(na)katarR^itvaM kiM vochchAraNamAtram.h | Adye pauruSheyatvApattiH | dvitIye sArvaj~nyAsiddhiH | upAdhyAya(Adi)vat.h | rajjau bhujaN^gavad.hbrahmaNyAropito veda iti chet.h | kathaM tarhi pANinyAdidR^iShyAntaH | nahi pANinAvAropitaM vyAkaraNam.h | kathaM chaivaM sati sArvaj~nyasiddhiH | tasyaiva vij~nAnashakttivivartatvAchChAstrasyeti chet.h(na) | viyadAdInAmapi prakAshashakttiprasaN^gAt.h | avidyAgatAvaraNAdishaktterapi brahmaNi tAttvikatvaprasaN^gAt.h(cha) | kiJNcha vede j~nAnakaraNatvashakttirbrahmaNi cha tatkartR^itvashakttiriti kiM kena saN^gatam.h | kutra chedamupalabdhamAropyagatA shakttirAropAdhiShThAne vAstavIti | tasmAdapavyAkhyAnameva tadityuktta eva sUtrAtharH |

|| OM tattu samanvayAt.h OM || astu shAstraikasamadhigamyaM jagatkAraNam.h | tathA.api shAstrata evAnyeShAM harahiraNyagarbhAdInAM pradhAnAdInAM cha jagatkAraNatvapratIterativyApakamidaM lakShaNam.h | nacha tachChAstraM viShNuparamiti vAchyam.h | abhiyukttaiH shivAdiparatvena vyAkhyAtatvAt.h | yadyapi nAmAni sarvANItyAdishrutyA shivAdinAmnAM viShNau shakttimAtramavasIyate | tathA.api na tAtparye pramANamasti | yatparaH shabdaH sa shabdArtha iti hi nyAyaH | nacha shakttimAtreNa tAtparyaM kalpayituM yukttam.h | atiprasaN^gAt.h | anyatra tAtparya(sya cha) j~nApakamabhiyukttavyAkhyAnamastItyukttam.h | tasmAdalakShaNametadityAshaN^kaya parihR^itaM sUtrakR^itA tattu samanvayAditi |

tatrAnvayapadArthamAha- ta eveti || 
upakramAdaya evAnvIyante shakttitAtparyagochareNa sambaddhayante tathA j~nAyanta iti yAvat.h vAkyAnyetaiH ityanvayanAmAnaH | atropakramAdiprasiddhapadaM parityajya yaugikAnvayapadaparigrahaNene(heNe)daM sUchayati | na shAstratAtparyAvagatAvApAtapratItirvyAkhyAtR^ivachanaM vA liN^gam.h | kintUpakramAdaya eva | teShAmavyabhichAritvAt.h | pratItivyAkhyAnayostu vyabhichAritvAt.h | yatrApi pratIvyAkhyAne na vyabhicharatastatrApyupakramAdyanusandhAnapUrvakatvenaiva na tu svataH | ata upajIvyatvAdupakramAdInAmeva tAtparyaliN^gatvamiti | tadidamAha- ta eveti ||

tathAchaivaM sUtrayojanA | anvayAdupakramAdiliN^gasamudAyAt.h shAstre samyak.h pravichArite sati sarvashAstrasya bhagavatyeva samyagvachanavR^ittyA.anvayAchChakttitAtparyalakShaNasambandhAvagamAttadviShNvAkhyaM brahmaiva jagajjanmAdikAraNatvena shAstrayoni na tu harahiraNyagarbhAdaya iti | anantaguNaparipUrNatvaM hi pradhAnalakShaNam.h | tatra cha shAstraM pramANIkriyamANaM vachanavR^ittyA sarvameva cha yukttam.h | lakShaNAdinA vR^ittau vAchyArthaguNAlAbhAt.h | vAchye tadguNaprasaN^gAchcha | evaM katipayavAkyairanantaguNApratipAdanAt.h | vAkyAntaraviShayasya cha tadguNa(va)ttvaprasaN^gAchcha | ataH saMshabdasyAvR^ittirupapannA |

tathAhi | "yato vAcho nivartante' "ashabdamasparsham.h' ityAdishruteH, "shabdo na yatra purukArakavAn.h' ityAdismR^iteshcha brahma avAchyamavasIyate | vachanavR^ittishcha dravyaguNakriyAjAtinimittA | nacha brahmaNo dravyAdiyogo.asti | "kevalo nirguNashcha'"niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntam.h' ityAdyAgamAt.h | tatkathaM tasya vAchyatA sambhavati | aupaniShadatvaM (tu) cha lakShaNayA vR^ittyA sambhavanna vAchyatAmapekShate | ato.avAchyatvAdbrahmaNo na vachanavR^ittyA shAstragamyatvamiti | apara Aha na sarvashAstrapratipAdyatvaM brahmaNaH sambhavati nishchayopAyAbhAvAt.h | upakramAdayo hi tannishchayopAyAH | taishchAsmadAdyadhigatashAstrasya kathaJNchidbrahmaviShayatAvadhAraNe.apyasmadanadhigatashAstrasya tatparatAvadhAraNAyogAt.h | "anantA vai vedAH' iti shruteranantaM hi shAstramavagamyate | nachAnantashAstrAdhigamo.asmAkaM kalpakoTishatairapi sambhavati | viphalashcha shAstraikadeshasya brahmaparatvAdhyavasAyaH | ekadeshAntare tadviparItapratipAdanasyApi shaN^kanAt.h | nacha vastuni vikalpaH sambhavati iti atrApi sandehaH samAskandati, ityato na sarvashAstraprAmANyAjjagajjanmAdikAraNaM samastaguNaparipUrNaM brahma siddhayati | ityevaM prApte avAchyatvashaN^kAM tAvannirAchaShye sUtrakAraH- IkShaternAshabdamiti ||
