atra IkShateriti dhAtunirdeshaH | na chAvivakShitArthaM shabdamAtraM brahmaNo vAchyatve heturbhavitumarhatIti tadartho.anenopalakShyate | nacha brahmAsambandhIkShaNamapyatra heturbhavati atiprasaN^gAt.h | sambandhashcha na kartR^itvAdirUpaH shrutyananugamAt.h vipakShe bAdhakAbhA(vAchcha)vaprasaN^gAchcha | ata IkShaNaM brahmakarmakameva hetutvena vAchyam.h | nachaitadapi yukttam.h vyadhikaraNatvaprasaN^gAt.h | tasmAdIkShaNakarmatvameva hetutayA vivakShitam.h ityAshayenokttam.h- IkShaNIyatvata iti ||
tadityanuvartate | tena viShNurityAha | na vidyate vAchakaH shabdo yasya tadashabdam.h | avAchyamityarthaH | vAchyamiti vakttavye nAvAchyamiti vachanaM "dvau naJNau prakR^itamarthaM sAtishayaM gamayataH' iti vachanAdavadhAraNArthamityabhipretyokttaM- vAchya eveti || nanvavadhAraNamapi kimartham.h | uchyate | tattvanirNayAtharM hi nyAyasUtram.h | nirNayashcha svaparapakShasAdhanopalambhAbhyAmeva bhavati | nAnyataramAtreNa | yathokttam.h | vimR^ishya pakShapratipakShAbhyAmarthAvadhAraNaM nirNaya iti | tadatrAvadhAraNe kR^ite vAchyatvavidhiravAchyatvaniShedhashchetyubhayamapi shrutyarthAbhyAM pratij~nAtaM syAt.h | ubhayasAdhanArthashchekShaNIyatvaheturvij~nAyate | tathAcha nirNayo bhavet.h | vAchyamiti tu pratij~nAte parapakShapratiShedho na kR^itaH syAt.h | nacha tadarthamanyatsUtramasti | ato yuktto.ayaM nirdeshaH | evamanyatrApi veditavyam.h | 
idamukttaM bhavati | brahma vAchyaM bhavitumarhati, na punaravAchyamIkShaNakarmatvAdghaTavat.h | IkShaNIyatvaM cha brahmaNaH "sa etasmAjjIvadhanAtparAtparaM purishayaM puruShamIkShate' "AtmanyevAtmAnaM pashyet.h' ityAdishrutisiddhamiti | 
nanu brahmaNo vAchyatvAbhAve kiM bAdhakam.h | IkShaNIyatvaM na syAt.h | tathAcha brahmaj~nAnAbhAvena shAstravaiyarthyamanirmokShashcha syAditi chenna | vAchyatvasyAvyApakatvAdIkShaNIyatvasyAvyApyatvAchcha | nahyavyApakanivR^ittiravyApyanivR^ittimApAda(yati)yituM shaknoti | IkShaNIyatvaM hi pratyakShAnumAnAgamatadAbhAsanimittaM vyApakaM yukttam.h | vAchyatvaM cha shabdavR^ittivisheShopAdhikaM vyApyameveti | maivam.h | na tAvadidaM mokShArthamupadiShyaM brahmekShaNaM pramANAbhAsajanyam.h | bhrAnteravidyAnivartakatvAbhAvAt.h | nApi pratyakShAnumAnajam.h | shAstraikasamadhigamyatAyAH sAdhitatvAt.h | tathAcha prakArAntarAbhAve sati yadi brahma vAchyamapi na bhavettadekShaNIyamapi na bhavediti bAdhakaM sambhavatyeva | nacha vyAptya(bhA)sambhavaH | vyatirekasambhavAt.h | yat.h yatkArakAviShayaH tat.h tatkriyA.aviShayaH yathA kuThArAdyaviShayo gaganaM na ChidAviShaya iti sAmAnyavyAptisambhavAchcha | 
nanu mAbhUtpramANAbhAsaiH pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAM chaikShaNaM brahmaNaH, mA cha bhUdvAchyam.h, tathA.api shabdalakShyatayekShaNIyaM cha bhaviShyati, tathAcha vipakShe bAdhakAbhAvAdaprayojako hetuH, ityata Aha- na cheti || 
hi yasmAdanyathA vAchyatvAbhAve lakShyatvaM kvApi na dR^iShyam.h | tasmAdavAchyatve brahmaNo lakShyatvA(yogA)bhAvAllakShaNayA.api nekShaNIyatvamiti sheShaH | kenachichChabdena vAchyameva hi tIrAdikaM kenachillakShyaM dR^iShyamiti |

IkShateH | tadaikShata bahusyAM prajAyeyeti, tattejo.asR^ijata' "i aikShata lokAnusR^ijA iti, sa imAMllokAnasR^ijata', "sa IkShAM chakre, sa prANamasR^ijata' itIkShitR^itvashravaNAtkAraNasya | syAdevam.h | yadi sUtrakAraH shabdAnAM brahmaNi lakShaNAmabhipreyAt.h | na chaitadasti | yadi sUtrakAro brahmaNi shabdAnAM lakShaNAmabhipraiti | tadA kathaM samanvayaM brUyAt.h | kintvanvayamAtraM brUyAt.h | samanvayaM chAbravIt.h | tena j~nAyate na lakShaNA sUtrakArasyAbhipretA kiM nAma mukhyavR^ittireveti |

samIchIno (hi) anvayaH samanvayaH | sacha shabdasya vAchyArtha eva ghaTate | tatraiva sAkShAchChakttimattvAt.h | lakShyArthe tu vAchyAthardvAreNAnvayo na samIchInaH | ataH samanvayashabdaM prayuJNjAnena sUtrakR^itA vAchyavAchakabhAva eva pratij~nAta iti j~nAyate | sa chAvAchyatvashaN^kAnirAsamantareNa sarvathA.apyasambhAvitaH syAditi vAchyatvasamarthanameva prAthamikamiti | idaM chAbhyupagamyokttam.h  | lakShaNAvAde.anvaya eva nopapadyate | kutaH samanvayaH | samIchInatA tu tAtparyavattA | sA cha lAkShaNike.apyarthe shabdAnAM sambhavatIti na samanvayasiddhayarthaM vAchyatvaM samarthanIyamiti chenna | saMshabdasArthAntaraM vyAkhyAyAmapi jaghanyavR^ittyA lakShaNayA samanvayAshrayaNanibandhe kAraNAbhAvAt.h | 
nanvasti kAraNam.h | tattu samanvayAditi nirguNe hi brahmaNi samanvayaH sUtrakR^itA pratij~nAtaH | na cha tatra shabdAnAM vachanavR^ittiH sambhavati | tasyA dravyAdisambandhanibandhanatvAt.h | nirguNe cha tadabhAvAt.h | ato j~nAyate lakShaNA.a.ashritA sUtrakR^iteti | evaMcha sati saMshabdasyApyuktta evArtho nishchIyata iti | syAdapyevam.h | yadi nirguNe samanvayaH pratij~nAtaH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | tathA hi kimatra nirguNasya prakR^itatvAttaditi tatparAmarsho.aN^gIkriyate | uta saguNasya prakR^itatve.api tatparAmarshAsambhavena jahadajahallakShaNayA nirguNaparAmarsho.abhyupeyate | AdyaM dUShayati- janmAdIti ||

unmattaM vyAhatabhAShiNam.h |

tvAmapavyAkhyAtAraM shrutiyukttibhyAM bad.hdhvA nirAkR^ityAsmachChAstraM vedaM sUtrasUchitAbhiH shrutibhiryukttibhishchAJNjasA nairantaryeNa sAdaraM cha shiShyairvichArayAma iti | anenedamuditaM bhavati | yAvadApAtaramaNIyaM pareShAM vyAkhyAnaM shiShyAH pashyeyuH, na tAvadasmaduktte sUtrANAM nijArthe.apyaJNjasA.a.adaraM kuryuH | kimasau sUtrArthaH kiM vA.ayamiti sandehAvaskandanAt.h | nirAkR^ite tvapavyAkhyAne nairantaryAdarAbhyAmasmadukttameva (sUtrA)arthamupAdAya shAstrArthamImAMsAyAM nirvichikitsAH pravatareran.h | ato mA(nAma)bhUdayaM sUtrArthastathA.api sUtrArthagrahaNopAyatvAdvayAkaraNAdAvudAharaNapratyudAharaNapradarshanAdivanna kaJNchana doShamAvahati | kiM nAma guNahetureva bhavatIti |

| mukhyAtikrameNAmukhyaprayoge kiM prayojanamiti chet.h | syAdayaM prayojanAnuyogo yadyayaM svatantraprayogaH syAt.h | naitadasti | rUDhatvAt.h yathokttam.h, "rUDhopachAro rUDhalakShaNopachAro lakShaNA' iti | anyo.apyAha "mukhyArthabAdhe tadyoge rUDhito.atha prayojanAt.h' iti | tadidamAha- avAchyamiti ||

|| OM Anandamayo.abhyAsAt.h OM ||  athAto brahmajij~nAseti yasya brahmaNo jij~nAsA vihitA tatsvarUpaM janmAdyasya yataH shAstrayonitvAditi lakShaNapramANAbhyAM svetarasamastavastuvyAvR^ittatayA.avadhAritam.h | pramANasyAnyaparatvashaN^kayA lakShaNasyAtivyAptiH samanvayasUtreNa parihR^itA | brahmaNashcha sakalashAstrapramANakatvAsambhAvanAshaN^kekShatyadhikaraNe nirAkR^itA | nahi lakShaNapramANanirUpaNavyatirekeNa vastuvichAraNaM nAmAsti | sambhAvanayA tu na varatvavadhAraNArthA | apramANatvAt.h | kintu yiAsambhAvanayA samIchInayorapi lakShaNapramANayeratathAbhAvashaN^kayA pravR^ittisaN^kochastatraiva sambhAvanopayogaH | vastutastu lakShaNapramANAbhyAmeva vastuvyavasthetyato brahmasvarUpanirUpaNe.avasheShAbhAvAtkimAnandamayo.abhyAsAdityAdinA.adhyAyenetyAshaN^kayAdhyAyasheShasya kR^ityamAha- evamiti ||

satyam.h | na brahmasvarUpanirUpaNe kimapyavashiShyam.h | tathA.api tattu samanvayadityupakramAditAtparyaliN^gabalAtsakalasyApi shAstrasya yo brahmaNi paramamukhyayA vR^ittyA pratipAdyapratipAdakatvalakShaNasamanvayo.abhihitastameva samanvayaM vibhAgena prapaJNchenAnandamaya ityAdinA.adhyAyena vadati sUtrakAra iti na vaiyarthyam.h | tattu samanvayAditi hi pratij~nAmAtreNokttam.h | tadyAvadudAharaNatvena vAkyavisheShAnupAdAya vimarshapUrvakaM pUrvottarapakShopAlambhasAdhanAbhyAM na prapaJNchyate tAvadanukttaprAyamarkAkAritvAt.h | anyathA paro.api hyanyadeva samanvayAdityuktavA kR^itI syAt.h | yadi hi pratyayamanutpAdyaiko.ayaM bhUmadhyapradesha iti brUyAt.h | tadA paro.api kiM na brUyAtparastAdvitasteriti | tasmAdAvashyakaM samanvayaprapaJNchanam.h | tadanena samanvayasUtreNAdhyAyasheShasya prapaJNchyaprapaJNchakabhAvena saN^gatirdarshitA | evaM tarhi tadAnantaryameva syAtkutovyavadhAnamityata ukttamevamiti | evamIkShatyadhikaraNavyutpAditanyAyena brahmaNaH shAstrAvagamyatve mukhyayA vR^ittyA sakalashAstrapratipAdyatve sambhAvite satIti | etadukttaM bhavati | satyaM prapaJNchanamanantaraprAptam.h tathA.apyavAchyatvAdyAshaN^kAnirAsena shAstrAvagamyatvasambhAvanAsamarthanena vyavadhIyate | sati hi tasminna(nneta)syAvasaraH | shabdaleshasaJNchArAsambhave vAkyatAtparyavichArasyAnavakAshatvAt.h | nahi toyAbhyavahArAsamarthasya mumUrShoH shaShkulIbhakShaNaM sachetanaH sambhAvayatIti | "svAdiShvasarvanAmasthAne' iti padasaMj~nA.anushAsanAdatra na yatibhaN^gashshaN^kanIyaH | 
mAyAvAdI tUttarasUtrasandarbhamAkShipya samAdhAnamAha | dvirUpaM hi brahmAvagamyate vedAntavAkyeShu | nAmarUpavikAropAdhivishiShyaM tadviparItaM cha sarvopAdhivivarjitam.h | "yatra hi "dvaitamiva bhavati' "sarvANi rUpANi vichintya dhIraH' ityevaM sahasrasho.avidyAvidyAviShayabhedena brahmaNo dvirUpatAM darshayanti vedAntavAkyAni | tatrAvidyA.avasthAyAM brahmaNa upAsyopAsakAdilakShaNaH sarvo vyavahAraH | tatra kAnichidbrahmaNa upAsanAnyabhyudayAtharAni | kAnijikramamuktayarthAni kAnichitkarmasamR^iddhayarthAni | evamapekShitopAdhibhedaM brahmopAsyatvena nirastasamastopAdhi tu j~neyatvenopadishyata ityasyArthasya pradarshanAyettaragrantha Arabhyata iti | 
tadidamanupapannam.h | brahmaNo dvairUpyasyAprAmANikatvAt.h | sarvANyapi hi vedavAkyAnyasaN^khayeyakalyANaguNAkaraM sakaladoShagandhavidhuramekarUpameva brahma nArAyaNAkhyaM pratipAdayanti | kintu kAnichitsarvaj~natvasarveshvaratvasavarAntaryAmitvasaundaryaudAryavIryAdiguNavishiShyatayA | kAnichidapahatapApmatvanirduHkhatvaprAkR^itabhautikavigraharahitatvAdidoShAbhAvavishiShyatayA |  kAnichitadigahanatAj~nApanAya vAN^manasAgocharatvAdyAkAreNa | kAnichitsarvaparihAreNa tasyaivopAdAnAyAdvitIyatvena | kAnichitsarvasattApratItipravR^ittinimittatApratipattyarthaM sarvAtmakatvena ityevamAdyanekaprakAraiH paramapuruShaM bodhayanti | tato vyAkulabuddhayo gurusampradAyavikalA ashrutavedavyAkhyAtAraH sarvatrApyekarUpatAmananusandadhAnA vedaM Chindanti | na (cha)etad.hdvairUpyaprapaJNchanamuttaratropalabhyate | nApyasyAvidyAviShayasya prapaJNchanaM mokShashAstre.atropayujyate | prasaN^gAduchyata iti chenna | sarvasva prAsaN^gikatve pratipAdyAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | tadidamAbhANakaM laukikAnAM nAtivartate "sArthAdapi taskarA bahavaH' iti | etachcha saguNanirguNabhedaM nirAkurvatA.a.achAryeNa nirastamiti neha punaH prakrAntam.h | tathAcha bhAShyam.h | nAnyathA tadadR^iShyeriti | 
nanvevamadhyAyasya samanvayapratipAdanalakShaNaikArthatvenaikavAkyatve sati pAdabhedaH kiMnibandhanaH | avAntarArthopAdhibhedAditi bhAvenAha- tatreti || 
chaturvidhA (hi) vaidikAH shabdAH | kechidbrahmaNyevaprasiddhAH | anye.anyatraprasiddhAH, kechidubhayatraprasiddhAH, apare tvanyatraivaprasiddhA iti | sarve.api pratyekaM nAmaliN^gAtmakatayA | dvividhAH | sAkShAddharmivAchino nAmAtmakAH | dharmadvArA dharmiNi vartamAnA liN^gAtmakAH | teShu brahmaNi prasiddhAnAM samanvayo na vakttavyaH | vivAdAbhAvAt.h | tatraiva cha mImAMsA.avatArAt.h | tatra vakttavyasamanvayeShu trividheShu shabdeShvanyatraprasiddhAnAM nAmAtmakAnAM shabdAnAM viShNAveva samanvayam.h | tatra prathame.adhyAye prathame pAde vadatyajaH | anyeShAmanyeShviti tatratatra vakShyati | kramaniyame tu heturupariShyAdvakShyate | prathame spaShyabrahmaliN^gAnAM dvitIyatR^itIyayoraspaShyabrahmaliN^gAnAM samanvayaH | chaturthe pradhAnasya shAbdatvanirAkaraNamityukttam.h |

nanvatra pAde saptAdhikaraNAni samanvayavibhAgArthAni | tatra saptAnAM shabdAnAM brahmaNi samanvayaH siddhayet.h | tatkathamanyatrasiddhAnAM nAmAtmakAnAM sarvashabdAnAM samanvayasiddhiratra syAt.h | anyathA samanvayasUtreNaivAlam.h | kimanenAtyalpaprapaJNchaneneti | maivam.h | ekaikatrAdhikaraNe samAnanyAyAnamanekashabdarAshInAM nirNIyamAnatvAt.h | vAkyavisheShagrahaNasya pUvarpakShavisheShopAdAnasya siddhAntapramANavisheShasvIkArasya chodAharaNArthatvAt.h | pratyekaM nirNaye shAstrasyAparyavasAnaprasaN^gaH | vishvatomukhatA cha sUtrANAM na syAt.h | tarhi nirNetavyashabdAvachChedakopAdhayo vakttavyAH | anyathA.asyedamudAharaNamiti j~nAtumashakyatvAt.h | sarvodAharaNatve cha sarvathA.adhikaraNAntarAnArambhaprasaN^gAditi | satyam.h | santi pratyadhikaraNaM nirNetavyArthAvachChedakopAdhaya ityAshayavAnAnandamayAdhikaraNanirNeyashabdopAdhimAha- guNIti || 
AnandamayAdishabdA hi guNisAmAnyaM vadanti | na shatakratvAdishabdebhya ivaitebhyo guNivisheShapratItirasti | te cha mayaT.hpratyayAdinA brahmaNe.anyatpratyAyayantIti bhavantyanyatraprasiddhAH | guNavAchinastvAnandAdayaste guNini brahmaNi vartituM nArhantItyanyatraprasiddhAH | guNaguNinorabhedastvahikuNDalAdhikaraNa eva sAkShAtsUtrakR^itA vakShyate | abhede.api shabdAdisAN^karyAbhAvashcheti | 
taittirIyake sa vA eSha puruSho.annarasamaya ityadinA.annamayaprANamayamanomayavij~nAnamayAnandamayAH paThyante | tatra saMshayaH | kimete.annamayAdayaH paramAtmaiva | uta tadanyaH kashchiditi | sarvatra brahmashabdashravaNAttasya cha viShNAvanyatra cha prayogAt.h | kiM tAvatprAptam.h | anya evAnnamayAdishabdArtha iti | kutaH | annamayAdishabdA hi vikaravAchinaH | mayaT.h pratyayasya vikArAthare.anushAsanAt.h | vikArasya cha sharIrAdikosheShu sambhavAt.h | sarvavikArAtmakatvena prakR^itau vopapatteH | jIvAnAM vA vikArAbhimAninAmannamayatvAdikaM yukttam.h | gauraH shyAma ityAdivat.h | adhiShThAtrINAM brahmAdidevatAnAM vA.ayaM shabdaH sambhavati | ashanirindra itivat.h | nacha vikAratvaM parasya brahmaNaH sambhavati | nirvikAro.akSharaH shuddha ityAdeH | yadyapi vikAra iva prAchurye.api mayaT.hpratyayo.asti | tathA.apyannamayashabdastAvadvikArArtho.aN^gIkAryaH | "oShadhIbhyo.annamannAtpuruShaH' ityoShadhijanitAnnavikAraM puruShashabdAbhidheyaM sharIraM prakR^itya "sa vA eSha puruSho.annamannarasamayaH' ityukttatvAt.h | "tasyedameva shiraH' ityaparokShatayA nirdeshAt.h | tathAcha dvaividhyakalpanA.anupapatteH sarvatra vikArArtha evAN^gIkAryaH | kiJNchAnnamayAdayaH paJNcha, brahma tvekameva, ataH kathaM tadetaiH shabdairuchyeta | api chaite parasparamanyatayA sharIrasharIribhAvenAntaratvena chochyante | nachaivaM brahma bhavitumarhati | nacha tarhyAnandamayo.astu brahma sarvAntaratvAditi vAchyam.h | vikArapravAhapatitatvAt.h | annamayAdyAntaratvamAtreNa sarvAntaratvAnishchayAt.h | kiJNcha brahmavidApnoti paramiti prakR^itaM paraM brahma Anandamayasya "brahma puchChaM pratiShThA' ityavayavatayA pratIyate | nachAvayava evAvayavI, virodhAt.h | ato na annamayAdayaH paJNchApi brahma kiM tvanya eveti | evaM prApte siddhAntayatsUtraM vyAkhyAti- samudrashAyinamiti || 
atra taittirIyake "anyAsu chatadUShAsu shAkhAsvapi sahasrashaH | Anandamaya ityAdyaiH shabdairvAchyo hariH svayam.h' ityetAvatA.a.anandamayo brahmeti pratij~nAbhAgo vyAkhyAtaH | tatra taittirIyaka ityudAharaNavAkyagrahaNam.h | anyAsviti nirNetavyavyapadeshaH | etadrUpAsviti guNisAmAnyaguNavAchinAmavatIShvityarthaH | tatra heturabhyAsAditi | tadvayAkhyAnaM ye.annamiti | "ye.annaM brahmopAsate, ye prANaM brahmopAsate, AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn.h, vij~nAnaM brahma chedveda, asadbrahmeti veda chet.h' ityannamayAdiviShayatayodAhR^iteShu shlokeShu brahmashabdasyAbhyAsAdityarthaH | ekaviShayAsakR^idukttirmukhyo.abhyAsaH | na chaivamatrAsti | kiM tvasakR^idakttimAtra(mitij~nApa)miti shaN^kAyAmekaviShayatA.apyastIti j~nApayitumityAderityanuktavA ityAdirUpAdityukttam.h | annamayAdiviShayatvena brahmashabdasya shrutatvAdityukttaM bhavati | brahmashabdena kathamayaM nishchaya ityata Aha- brahmashabdasyeti || tadapi kuta ityata Aha- shrutiriti || "tadeva brahma paramam.h' iti sAvadhR^itiH shrutiH viShNumeva brahmashabdavAchyaM jagau yato.ata iti yojanA | tatrApi taditi parAmarshaviShayo viShNuriti kuta ityata ukttam.h- samudrashAyinamiti || vyAkhyAtametatprathamasUtre | 
nanvAnandamaya ityeva sUtre pratij~nA, tatkathamAnandamaya ityAdyairiti vyAkhyAnamityata Aha- upalakShaNatvamiti ||
AnandamayashchAsau pUrvashcha sa eShAmasti ta AnandamayapUrviNasteShAm.h | syAdayaM vyAkhyAnavyAkhyeyayorvisaMvAdo yadyatrAnandamayashabdaH svamAtrasya grAhakaH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | kiM tvatrAnandamayashabdasya samAnanyAyAnAmannamayAdishabdAnAmupalakShaNakatvam.h | evamuttaratrApyAkAshAdishabdAnAmapi | svasamAnanyAyashabdAntaropalakShaNatvamavagantavyamiti | ajahallakShaNA chaiShA | tenAnandamayasya tyAgo na mantavyaH | ata eva vikArashabdAdityAdyAkShepANAM tatparihArANAM svatantrayukttInAM chopalakShaNatvaM draShyavyam.h | 
syAdetat.h | mukhyArthabAdhe tadyoge prayojane cha sati lakShaNA dR^iShyA | tadatra vAchakashabdaprayoge sambhavati kiM lAkShaNikashabdaprayoge prayojanaM sUtrakArasya | nacheyaM rUDhalakShaNA | yena prayojanAnapekShetyata Aha- sUtrasyeti ||
yadi mukhya eva prayogaH kriyate | tadA.annamayaprANamayamanomayavij~nAnamayAnandamayA ityeva prayokttavyaM syAt.h | tathAcha sUtrasyAlpAkSharatvalakShaNaM hIyeta | shrutyA.arthAdvA j~nAyamAnasyArthasyAvachanaM hyalpAkSharatvam.h | ayaM chArtho.arthojj~nAyata iti vakShyAmaH | ataH sUtrasyAlpAkSharatvena prayojanena lAkShaNikaprayogaH sUtrakArasyeti |
nanu sUtre yathAshrutameva ched.h gR^ihyate tadA kIdR^isho doSho yena lakShaNA vyAkhyAtavyetyata Aha- sarveti || pravR^ittatvAditi sheShaH | yadi hi sUtre shrutamAtraM gR^ihyeta tadA sUtrashatena vAkyashatasamanvaya eva siddhayet.h | natu sarvashAkhAnirNayaH | sarvashAkhAnirNayArthaM pravR^ittashani chaitAni | sUtrAntarAbhAvAt.h | ataH sarvashAkhAnirNAyakatvasyAnyathA.anupapattyA yathAshrutamAtraparityAgena lakShaNA vyAkhyeyeti gamyate | lakShaNA.a.ashrayaNe hi sarvashAkhAnirNayaH siddhayatIti | 
nanu yathA yathAshrutagrahaNe bAdhakamasti sUtrANAM vishvatomukhatvAsambhavaH tathopalakShaNA.a.ashrayaNe.api bAdhakasadbhAvaH samAnaH | AnandamayashabdenAnnamayAdInAmiva sarvashabdAnAmupalakShayituM shakyatvenottarAdhikaraNArambhAnupapatteriti chet.h | kiM samAnanyAyashabdAntaraviShayAdhikaraNAnArambhaprasaN^go bAdhakaH | kiMvA nyAyAntaraviShayashabdAntaragocharAdhikaraNAnarambhaprasaN^gaH | nAdyaH | iShyatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | vaiShamyAt.h | annamayAdayo hi samAnanyAyatayA sambandhenopalakShaNatayA gR^ihyante | taditareShAM tUpalakShaNAyAM kaH sambandhaH | nahi sambandhena vinA lakShaNA dR^iShyA | shabdatvena sandigdhatvena chopalakShaNamupaplavaH | tathA sati tattu samanvayAdityanenaiva pUrNatvAt.h | atha samAnanyAyaviShayatve.apyadhikaraNAntarArambho dR^ishyate | upalakShaNapakShe sa na syAdityApAdyata ityata Aha- punashcheti || tatra pUrvAdhikaraNavyutpAdinyAyaviShaye.apyarthe yadadhikaraNAntaramArabhyate tatpUrvAdhikaraNanyAyAchChAdakAdhikAshaN^kAlakShaNAtpunaradhikaraNAntarArambhaprApakAddhetorvidyamAnAdyujyate | idamukttaM bhavati | samAne.api nyAye punaradhikaraNAntarArambhAnyathA.anupapattyA yathAshruta eva sUtrArtha iti yadukttaM tanna | anyathopapatteH | adhikAshaN^kayA tannyAyaviShayatvAbhAve pareNAshaN^kite.adhikAshaN^kAnirAkaraNena punastannyAyaviShayatvapradarshanArthatvAdadhikaraNAntarArambhasya | vishvatomukhatvabhaN^gastu niravakAsha iti lakShaNA.a.ashrayaNameva nyAyyamiti | 
nanu sarvashAkhAnirNAyakatvamevaiShAM sUtrANAM nAsti | sarvashAkhAnAM kAryaniShThatvenAbrahmaviShayatvAt.h | brahmaniShThastu vedAntabhAgo.alpIyAn.h vinApi lakShaNA.a.ashrayaNena yathAshrutArthaiH sUtraiH shakyo nirNetumiti kiM lakShaNA.a.ashrayaNenetyata Aha- sarve vedA iti ||
sarveShAmapi vedAnAM brahmaniShThatAmAheti sheShaH | 
yadyatropalakShaNamabhipretaM syAttadA prathamaprAptatvAdannamayashabdamevopAdadyAt.h | AnandamayashabdaM tUpAdadatsUtrakArastanmAtravivakShAM sUchayatItyata Aha- Anandamayeti ||
annamayAdInAmabrahmatve vikArashabdaH sAdhAraNopapattiH | AnandamayarUpe tu brahmavidApnoti paramityukttasya "brahma puchChaM pratiShThA' iti puchChatvoktayA samastasyAvayavina AnandamayasyAbrahmatvaprAptiradhikA.apyupapattirastItyato.atrAviIhatairbhavitavyamiti j~nApayitumAnandamayanAma gR^ihItaM sUtrakR^itetyanyathopapattirukttA bhava(tI)ti | yadyAnandamayo brahma syAttadA tadavayavasya samastAyA mukhyAyA AbrahmatAyAH samyagbrahmatAyA aprApteriti vA | tatashcha tadvedanAtparaprAptiH shrutA bAdhyeteti | nanvannamaye.apyadhikA.anupapattirasti | "oShadhIbhyo.annam.h | annAtpuruShaH | sa vA eSha puuruSho.annarasamayaH' iti | "tasyedameva shiraH' iti cha | maivam.h | asyApi vikAropapAdakatvena tadantarbhAvAt.h | yadvA athAto brahmajij~nAseti jij~nAsyatayokttasya brahmaNaH puchChatvoktayA samastAbrahmatAprApterAnandamayavichArasya prakR^itena saN^gatatvAdAnandamayanAmagrahaNamiti yojyam.h | 
nanu sUtrANAmupalakShaNatvAbhAve sarvashAkhAnirNayAbhAvaprasaN^genAstUpalakShaNatvam.h | AnandamayashabdasyAnnamayAdyupalakShaNatvamityayaM visheShaH kuta ityata Aha- brahmashabdasyeti ||
Anandamayasya brahmatve hi hetutvena(yo) brahmashabdAbhyAso.abhihitaH so.annamayAdiShvapi samAnaH | tathAchAnnamayAdInAmabrahmatve.anaikAntikaH kathamAnandamayasyApi brahmatvaM sAdhayet.h | ato.annamayAdisAdhAraNaM brahmashabdAbhyAsaM hetutvena vadatA sUtrakAreNa teShAmapi pakShatvamaN^gIkR^itamiti j~nAyate | chashabdena "asminnasya cha tadyogaM shAstItyAdihetUnAmapi sAdhAraNyaM sUchayati | AdigrahaNAdAnandAdInAM grahaNam.h | tasmAduktta eva sUtrArtha iti | 
nanvAnandamayasya kathaM brahmatvam.h | brahma puchChamiti brahmaNastatpuchChatvAbhidhAnAt.h | nacha brahmashabdo.anyaparaH | tathA satyatraivAnaikAntyApatteH | nacha nirapavAdo brahmashabdo hetuH na brahmashabdamAtramiti vAchyam.h | brahma puchChamityatrApyapavAdAbhAvAt.h | brahmAvayavatvamiti chenna | adyApyAnandamayasya brahmatvAsiddheriti | atra praShyavyam.h | kimavayavasya pUrNatve.avayavinaH pUrNatvaM nopapadyata ityabhiprAyaH | kiM vA.a.anandamasyAvayavinaH pUrNatve tadavayavasya pUrNatvAbhAvApAdanam.h | utAvayavAvayavinorbhedAdavayavasya ramAtmatvepa nAvayavinastattvamiti |

yadA.avayave.api brahmatA tathA satyavayavini sA svato.anAyasena syAt.h | avayavino.avayavApekShayA mahattvasya dR^iShyatvAt.h | tatashchAvayavasya pUrNatve.avayavinaH pUrNatvAnupapattiriti viruddhametat.h |

nanvatrAnnamayAdishabdAH shrUyante | uttaratra (tu) mayaT.hpratyayahInA annAdishabdA eva | shabdabhede cha nimittabhedenAbhidheyabhedena chAvashyaM bhavitavyam.h | na chAnnamayAdishabdA annAdishabdaparyAyA iti yukttam.h | pratyayArthasyAdhikasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | nacha bhImaseno bhImo balabhadro balaH satyabhAmA satyA punarnavA navA, kAchamAchI mAchItyAdivatsyAditi vAchyam.h | vaiShamyAt.h | bhImAdishabdA hi pratyekaM tadvAchakAH | na chAnnashabdamAtramannamayasya vAchakam.h | pratyayasya svArthikatvaprasaN^gAt.h | prAchuryArthashcha mayaDityukttam.h | nahyannamayo yaj~na iti vakttavye.annashabdamAtraM prayujyate | tasmAttatrAtra cha pR^ithagvastupratipAdanAtkathaM tatsaMvAdenAtrApi brahmapratipAdanamityuchyate | kiM tvatrAnnamayAdayaH koshAstatra tu brahmetyata Aha- prApyatveneti ||

adhIhyadhyApaya | NyarthasyAntarNItatvAt.h | bhagavo bhagavan.h | matuvaso ruH sambuddhau ChandasIti vachanAt.h | uktto bhR^iguNA pR^iShyo varuNaH "bhR^igurvai vAruNiH | varuNaM pitaramupasasAra | adhIhi bhagavo brahmeti | tasmA etatprovAcha | annaM prANaM chakShuHshrotraMmanovAcham.h' ityevaM brahmaprashnottaratvenokttatvAdannAdikaM brahmaiva bhavitumarhatItyarthaH | nanu tatra mayaTo.ashravaNAdbhinnaviShayatvamiti chenna | ukttottaratvAt.h | kiJNcha yathA satyannamayAdInpratyudAhR^itashlokeShu mayaTo.ashravaNAdbhinnaviShayatvaM syAt.h | astviti chenna | tathA sati tadudAharaNasyAsaN^gatiprasaN^gAt.h | yasyAnnAdervikArAstetatprashaMsAparatayA saN^gatistviti chenna | manomayashloke tadayogAt.h | tarhi tata evAnupapatterannAdishabdairannamayAdaya evochyata iti kalpyata iti chet.h | tarhyatrApi prakaraNavashAdannamayAdaya evochyanta ityaN^gIkAryam.h | uktte.athare hi saMvAditveneyamAkhyAyikokttA | tasmAdannamayAdaya evAtrochyante | te cha brahmaprashnottaratvenokttatvAnyathA.anupapattyA brahmaiveti | yadyapi "saiShA bhArgavI vAruNakSha vidyA parame vyomanpratiShThitA' iti sAkShAdbrahmavidyAtvamuchyate | tathA.api mImAMsArthaM yuktayupanyAsaH | athavA | asyApi samAnayogakShematvAditi |

brahmaiva vakttavyam.h | na punaryatkiJNchit.h | abodhe.api punaH punaH tadeva shabdAntareNa vakttavyam.h | dvAraM cha dvAratayaiva vakttavyam.h | natu tadAtmakatvena | nahi dhUmo.agnyAtmakatvena pradashyarte | chandradyudAharaNamapyasiddhameveti | AgamA vedAH | sampradAyavidaH smR^itItihAsapurANakartAraH | api chAvitaretarasamuchchayArthau | tarhi upadeshaprakArAj~natayA varuNo.anyadupadishatItyastu | maivam.h | lokapAlasyaitAvajj~nAnAbhAvasambhavAdityAshayena dvAropadeshashaN^kAnirAkaraNamupasaMharati- taditi ||

nanu varuNenoktteShvannAdiShvannaprANamanAMsi santu brahmasvarUpANi | annAdishabdAnAmattR^itvAdyarthatayA.anupapattyabhAvAt.h | chakShuHshrotravAkshabdaM tu kathaM brahma syAt.h | chakShurAdishabdAnAM chaShye.aneneti chakShuH | shR^iNotyaneneti shrotram.h | vadatyanayeti vAgiti karaNArthatvAt.h | brahmaNashcha karaNatvAnupapatteriti chenna | kartaryapi tad.hvyutpattisambhavAdityAha- chaShya iti ||

guNisAmAnyavAchinAM guNavAchinAM cha shabdAnAM samanvayAya pravR^itte.apyadhikaraNe.adhikaraNasiddhAntanyAyena siddhamapyarthAntaramupasaMharati- adhyAtmagaishcheti || ata eva nAdhikaraNopakramavirodha iti | 
samastairguNisAmAnyavAchakairguNavAchakairadhyAtmaviShayaiH(cha) prANavAgAdibhiradhibhUtaviShayaishchAnnauShadhyAdibhishshabdairbhagavAneva mukhyatayodita ityupasaMhAro nopapadyate | asyArthasya prAganukttatvAt.h | nanUkttamupalakShaNaparo.ayamAnandamayashabda iti | satyam.h | upalakShaNaM hi prakR^itopayukttasyopapanyasya chArthasya bhavati | anyathA.atiprasaN^gAt.h | nachaiteShAM sarvashabdAnAM mukhyayA vR^ittyA bhagavadekavAchitvasamarthanaM prakR^itopayukttaM nApyupapannam.h | tathAhi | janmAdyasya yata iti sUtre jagajjanmAdikAraNatvAdInyaShyau lakShaNAni brahmaNo.abhihitAni | tatraiva shAstraM pramANamukttaM tR^itIyasUtre | samanvayasUtre cha teShAmeva vAkyAnAM brahmaNi samanvayaH pratij~nAtaH | ato jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM yatrayatra pratIyate teShAmeva vAkyAnAM parameshvare samanvayasamatharnaM prakR^itasaN^gatam.h | na sarveShAm.h | sarvatra jagajjanmAdikAraNatvapratipAdanAbhAvAt.h | kiJNcha yanniShThatayA jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM pratIyate tadvAchinaH shabdasya yayA kayAchana vR^ittyA bhagavatparatve samarthite.api lakShaNasyAtivyAptiH patihriyata eva | nahi gaN^gApadalakShyasya tIrasya ghoShAvAsatvaM na siddhayati | ato mukhyavR^ittisamarthanasya kvopayogaH | nopapadyate cha sarvashabdAnAM bhagavatyeva mukhyavR^ittisamarthanam.h | rUDhiyogau hi mukhyavR^ittI | tatrApi yogAdrUDhirbalavatI | nacha shabdAnAM bhagavati rUDhirasti | kintu taditaratraiva | yogastu sambhavati | tathA.api sa taditarasamAnaH | tathA chArthAntara eva mukhyavR^ittayaH shabdAH | rUDheryogasya cha sattvAt.h | neshvare | yogamAtrasya kathaJNchitsambhavAt.h | ataH sUtrakArasya sakalashabdAnAM mukhyayA vR^ittyA bhagavatyeva samanvayasamarthane saN^gatyupapattyorabhAvAdapavyAkhyAnametadityAshaN^kaya saN^gatiM tAvaddarshayati- janmAdIti || 
athAto brahmajij~nAseti prathamasUtre brahmashabdena jij~nAsyasya sakalaguNapUrNatvaM jIvAdivyAvR^ittyarthamupAttam.h | janmAdyasya yata iti dvitIyasUtreNa tatsiddhaye jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM brahmaNo lakShaNaM prokttam.h | ataH sUtradvayena sAdhyatayA sAdhakatayA chAnandAdisakalaguNapUrNatvaM jagajjanmAdikAraNatvaM cha prakR^itamiti | vivR^itaM chaitatpUrvamasmAbhiH | kimato yadyevamityata Aha- shAstramUlamiti || 
tadubhayaM pradhAnamapradhAnaM cha lakShaNamanumAnAdinA.ativyAptau shaN^kitAyAM tannivR^ittyarthaM tR^itIyasUtre shAstramUlaM shAstraikapramANamukttaM yatastatashchaturthe sUtre shAstrasyAnyaparatvashaN^kAyAM sarvashabdAnAM bhagavatyanvayaH pratij~nAtumuchito na katipayashabdAnAmiti sheShaH | sarvaguNapUrNatve shAstrasya pramANatayA.abhidhAne.api kutaH sarvashabdasamanvayaH pratij~nAtavya ityata Aha- anvaya iti || 
yataH sarvashabdAnAmanvaya eva guNasarvasvavedako na katipayashabdAnAm.h | ataH sarvashAstrAd.h guNasarvasvasiddhaye sa eva pratij~nAtavya iti sambandhaH | anyathA yasyaiva shabdasya samanvayo na pratij~nAyate tadartho guNo bhagavati na siddhayedativyAptishcha syAt.h | pratij~nAte cha samanvayasUtreNa
